00101 PdbFile::PdbFile(const std::string &pdb_file)
00102 {
00103     path_ = pdb_file;
00104     header_ = NULL;
00105     title_ = NULL;
00106     compound_ = NULL;
00107     number_of_models_ = NULL;
00108     model_type_ = NULL;
00109     residues_sequence_ = NULL;
00110     residue_modification_ = NULL;
00111     heterogens_ = NULL;
00112     heterogens_name_ = NULL;
00113     heterogen_synonyms_ = NULL;
00114     formulas_ = NULL;
00115     helixes_ = NULL;
00116     sheets_ = NULL;
00117     disulfide_bonds_ = NULL;
00118     links_ = NULL;
00119     sites_ = NULL;
00120     crystallography_ = NULL;
00121     origins_ = NULL;
00122     scales_ = NULL;
00123     matrices_ = NULL;
00124     models_ = NULL;
00125     connectivities_ = NULL;
00126     serial_number_mapping_ = PdbFile::PdbSerialNumberMapping();
00127     sequence_number_mapping_ = PdbFile::PdbSequenceNumberMapping();
00128     
00129     std::ifstream in_file;
00130     if(std::ifstream(pdb_file.c_str()))
00131     {
00132         cout << "Opening PDB file ..." << endl;
00133         in_file.open(pdb_file.c_str());
00134     }
00135     else
00136     {
00137         throw PdbFileProcessingException(__LINE__, "PDB file not found");
00138     }
00139 
00140     string line = "";
00141     string temp = "";
00142     stringstream ss;
00143     while(!in_file.eof())
00144     {
00145         if(!getline(in_file, line))
00146             break;
00147         else
00148         {
00149             temp = line.substr(0,6);
00150             temp = Trim(temp);
00151             if(temp.find("END") != string::npos || temp.compare("END") == 0)
00152                 break;
00153             else if(!line.empty())
00154                 ss << line << endl;
00155         }
00156     }
00157     in_file.close();
00158     if(temp.find("END") == string::npos || temp.compare("END") != 0)
00159     {
00160         std::ofstream out_file;
00161         out_file.open(pdb_file.c_str());
00162         out_file << ss.str() << "END";
00163         out_file.close();
00164     }
00165     else
00166     {
00167         std::ofstream out_file;
00168         out_file.open(pdb_file.c_str());
00169         out_file << ss.str() << temp;
00170         out_file.close();
00171     }
00172     in_file.open(pdb_file.c_str());
00173     if(!Read(in_file))
00174     {
00175         throw PdbFileProcessingException(__LINE__, "Reading PDB file exception");
00176     }
00177     in_file.close();            /// Close the parameter files
00178 }

00306 PdbFile::PdbPairVectorAtomNamePositionFlag PdbFile::GetAllResidueNames()
00307 {    
00308     PdbPairVectorAtomNamePositionFlag residue_names;
00309     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
00310     PdbModel* model = (*models.begin()).second;
00311     PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
00312     PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
00313     for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
00314     {
00315         PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
00316         PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
00317         for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
00318         {
00319             PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
00320             int dist = distance(atoms.begin(), it2);
00321             string atom_residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
00322             if(dist == 0)
00323             {
00324                 pair<string, string> pair_residue_position = make_pair(atom_residue_name, "S");
00325                 if(find(residue_names.begin(), residue_names.end(), pair_residue_position) == residue_names.end())
00326                         residue_names.push_back(pair_residue_position);
00327             }
00328             else if(dist == atoms.size() - 1)
00329             {
00330                 pair<string, string> pair_residue_position = make_pair(atom_residue_name, "E");
00331                 if(find(residue_names.begin(), residue_names.end(), pair_residue_position) == residue_names.end())
00332                     residue_names.push_back(pair_residue_position);
00333             }
00334             pair<string, string> pair_residue_position = make_pair(atom_residue_name, " ");
00335             if(find(residue_names.begin(), residue_names.end(), pair_residue_position) == residue_names.end())
00336                 residue_names.push_back(pair_residue_position);
00337         }
00338     }
00339     PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00340     for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
00341     {
00342         PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
00343         PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00344         for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
00345         {
00346             PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
00347             string atom_residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
00348             pair<string, string> pair_residue_position = make_pair(atom_residue_name, " ");
00349             if(find(residue_names.begin(), residue_names.end(), pair_residue_position) == residue_names.end())
00350             {
00351                 residue_names.push_back(pair_residue_position);
00352             }
00353         }
00354     }
00355     return residue_names;
00356 }

00398 PdbFile::PdbResidueVector PdbFile::GetAllResidues()
00399 {
00400     PdbFile::PdbResidueVector residues;
00401     map<string, bool> inserted_residues;
00402     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
00403     PdbModel* model = (*models.begin()).second;
00404     PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
00405     PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
00406     for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
00407     {
00408         PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
00409         PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
00410         for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
00411         {
00412             PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
00413             string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
00414             char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
00415             int sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
00416             char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
00417             char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
00418             stringstream ss;
00419             ss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
00420             string key = ss.str();
00421             if(!inserted_residues[key])
00422             {
00423                 PdbResidue* res = new PdbResidue(residue_name, chain_id, sequence_number, insertion_code, alternate_location);
00424                 residues.push_back(res);
00425                 inserted_residues[key] = true;
00426             }
00427         }
00428     }
00429     PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00430     for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
00431     {
00432         PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
00433         PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00434         for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
00435         {
00436             PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
00437             string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
00438             char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
00439             int sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
00440             char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
00441             char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
00442             stringstream ss;
00443             ss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
00444             string key = ss.str();
00445             if(!inserted_residues[key])
00446             {
00447                 PdbResidue* res = new PdbResidue(residue_name, chain_id, sequence_number, insertion_code, alternate_location);
00448                 residues.push_back(res);
00449                 inserted_residues[key] = true;
00450             }
00451         }
00452     }
00453     return residues;
00454 }

00490 PdbFile::PdbAtomVector PdbFile::GetAllAtomsOfResidue(PdbResidue *residue)
00491 {
00492     string target_residue_name = residue->GetResidueName();
00493     char target_residue_chain_id = residue->GetResidueChainId();
00494     int target_residue_sequence_number = residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
00495     char target_residue_insertion_code = residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
00496     char target_residue_alternate_location = residue->GetResidueAlternateLocation();
00497     stringstream ss;
00498     ss << target_residue_name << "_" << target_residue_chain_id << "_" << target_residue_sequence_number << "_" << target_residue_insertion_code << "_" << target_residue_alternate_location;
00499     string target_key = ss.str();
00500     
00501     PdbAtomVector atoms_of_residue;
00502     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
00503     PdbModel* model = (*models.begin()).second;
00504     PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
00505     PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
00506     for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
00507     {
00508         PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
00509         PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
00510         for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
00511         {
00512             PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
00513             string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
00514             char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
00515             int sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
00516             char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
00517             char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
00518             stringstream sss;
00519             sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
00520             string key = sss.str();
00521             if(target_key.compare(key) == 0)
00522             {
00523                 atoms_of_residue.push_back(atom);
00524             }
00525         }
00526     }
00527     PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00528     for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
00529     {
00530         PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
00531         PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00532         for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
00533         {
00534             PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
00535             string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
00536             char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
00537             int sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
00538             char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
00539             char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
00540             stringstream sss;
00541             sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
00542             string key = sss.str();
00543             if(target_key.compare(key) == 0)
00544             {
00545                 atoms_of_residue.push_back(atom);
00546             }
00547         }
00548     }
00549     return atoms_of_residue;
00550 }
00551 
00552 PdbFile::PdbResidueAtomsMap PdbFile::GetAllAtomsOfResidues()
00553 {
00554     PdbFile::PdbResidueAtomsMap residue_atom_map;
00555     map<string, bool> inserted_residues;
00556     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
00557     PdbModel* model = (*models.begin()).second;
00558     PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
00559     PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
00560     for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
00561     {
00562         PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
00563         PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
00564         for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
00565         {
00566             PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
00567             string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
00568             char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
00569             int sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
00570             char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
00571             char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
00572             stringstream ss;
00573             ss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
00574             string key = ss.str();
00575             if(!inserted_residues[key])
00576             {
00577                 residue_atom_map[key] = new vector<PdbAtom*>();
00578                 inserted_residues[key] = true;
00579             }
00580             residue_atom_map[key]->push_back(atom);
00581             
00582         }
00583     }
00584     PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00585     for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
00586     {
00587         PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
00588         PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00589         for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
00590         {
00591             PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
00592             string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
00593             char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
00594             int sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
00595             char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
00596             char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
00597             stringstream ss;
00598             ss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
00599             string key = ss.str();
00600             if(!inserted_residues[key])
00601             {
00602                 residue_atom_map[key] = new vector<PdbAtom*>();
00603                 inserted_residues[key] = true;
00604             }
00605             residue_atom_map[key]->push_back(atom);
00606         }
00607     }
00608     return residue_atom_map;
00609 }

00654             int sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
00655             char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
00656             char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
00657             stringstream ss;
00658             ss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
00659             string key = ss.str();
00660             if(!inserted_residues[key])
00661             {
00662                 residue_atom_map[key] = new vector<PdbAtom*>();
00663                 inserted_residues[key] = true;
00664                 key_order.push_back(key);

00666             residue_atom_map[key]->push_back(atom);

00672 PdbFileSpace::PdbAtom* PdbFile::GetAtomOfResidueByName(PdbResidue *residue, string atom_name, PdbFile::PdbResidueAtomsMap residue_atom_map)
00673 {
00674     string target_residue_name = residue->GetResidueName();
00675     char target_residue_chain_id = residue->GetResidueChainId();
00676     int target_residue_sequence_number = residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
00677     char target_residue_insertion_code = residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
00678     char target_residue_alternate_location = residue->GetResidueAlternateLocation();
00679     stringstream ss;
00680     ss << target_residue_name << "_" << target_residue_chain_id << "_" << target_residue_sequence_number << "_" << target_residue_insertion_code << "_" << target_residue_alternate_location;
00681     string target_key = ss.str();
00682     PdbAtomVector* atoms = residue_atom_map[target_key];
00683     
00684     for(PdbAtomVector::iterator it = atoms->begin(); it != atoms->end(); it++)
00685     {
00686         PdbAtom* atom = (*it);
00687         if(atom->GetAtomName().compare(atom_name) == 0)
00688             return atom;
00689     }
00690     return NULL;
00691 }

00706 PdbAtom* PdbFile::GetAtomOfResidueByAtomKey(string atom_key)
00707 {
00708     vector<string> key_tokens = Split(atom_key, "_");
00709     int serial_number = gmml::ConvertString<int>(key_tokens.at(1));
00710     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
00711     PdbModel* model = (*models.begin()).second;
00712     PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
00713     PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
00714     for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it = atom_cards.begin(); it != atom_cards.end(); it++)
00715     {
00716         PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it);
00717         PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atom_map = atom_card->GetAtoms();
00718         if(atom_map[serial_number] != NULL)
00719             return atom_map[serial_number];
00720     }
00721     PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00722     for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it++)
00723     {
00724         PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it);
00725         PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atom_map = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
00726         if(heterogen_atom_map[serial_number] != NULL)
00727             return heterogen_atom_map[serial_number];
00728     }
00729     return NULL;
00730 }

00756 vector<string> PdbFile::GetAllAtomNamesOfResidue(PdbResidue *residue, PdbFile::PdbResidueAtomsMap residue_atom_map)
00757 {
00758     string target_residue_name = residue->GetResidueName();
00759     char target_residue_chain_id = residue->GetResidueChainId();
00760     int target_residue_sequence_number = residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
00761     char target_residue_insertion_code = residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
00762     char target_residue_alternate_location = residue->GetResidueAlternateLocation();
00763     stringstream ss;
00764     ss << target_residue_name << "_" << target_residue_chain_id << "_" << target_residue_sequence_number << "_" << target_residue_insertion_code << "_" << target_residue_alternate_location;
00765     string target_key = ss.str();
00766     PdbAtomVector* atoms = residue_atom_map[target_key];
00767     
00768     vector<string> atom_names;
00769     for(PdbAtomVector::iterator it = atoms->begin(); it != atoms->end(); it++)
00770     {
00771         PdbAtom* atom = (*it);
00772         atom_names.push_back(atom->GetAtomName());
00773     }
00774     return atom_names;
00775 }

00777 vector<string> PdbFile::GetAllAtomNamesOfResidue(PdbResidue *residue)
00778 {
00779     PdbAtomVector atoms = GetAllAtomsOfResidue(residue);
00780     
00781     vector<string> atom_names;
00782     for(PdbAtomVector::iterator it = atoms.begin(); it != atoms.end(); it++)
00783     {
00784         PdbAtom* atom = (*it);
00785         atom_names.push_back(atom->GetAtomName());
00786     }
00787     return atom_names;
00788 }
00789 PdbFile::PdbPairVectorTerCardPositions PdbFile::GetAllTerCardPositions(vector<string> glycam_residue_names)
00790 {
00791     vector<pair<char, int> > ter_card_positions = vector<pair<char, int> >();
00792     // After residues that has no tails or has more than or equal two tails
00793     PdbFile::PdbResidueVector residues = this->GetAllResiduesFromAtomCard();
00794     for(PdbFile::PdbResidueVector::iterator it = residues.begin(); it != residues.end(); it++)
00795     {
00796         int dist = distance(residues.begin(), it);
00797         if(dist != residues.size() - 1)
00798         {
00799             PdbResidue* residue = (*it);
00800             string residue_name = residue->GetResidueName();
00801             if(find(glycam_residue_names.begin(), glycam_residue_names.end(), residue_name) != glycam_residue_names.end())
00802             {
00803                 // No tail || has more than or equal two tails
00804                 if(residue_name[0] == '0' || isalpha(residue_name[0]))
00805                 {
00806                     ter_card_positions.push_back(make_pair(residue->GetResidueChainId(), residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber() + 1));
00807                 }
00808             }
00809         }
00810     }
00811     return ter_card_positions;
00812 }

00952 
00953 void PdbFile::DeleteResidue(PdbResidue *residue)
00954 {
00955     string target_residue_name = residue->GetResidueName();
00956     char target_residue_chain_id = residue->GetResidueChainId();
00957     int target_residue_sequence_number = residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
00958     char target_residue_insertion_code = residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
00959     char target_residue_alternate_location = residue->GetResidueAlternateLocation();
00960     stringstream ss;
00961     ss << target_residue_name << "_" << target_residue_chain_id << "_" << target_residue_sequence_number << "_" << target_residue_insertion_code << "_" << target_residue_alternate_location;
00962     string target_key = ss.str();
00963     
00964     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
00965     for(PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap::iterator it = models.begin();it != models.end(); it++)
00966     {
00967         PdbModel* model = (*it).second;
00968         PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
00969         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
00970         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector updated_atom_cards = PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector();
00971         int serial_number = 1;
00972         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
00973         {
00974             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
00975             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
00976             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap updated_atoms = PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap();
00977             
00978             for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
00979             {
00980                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
00981                 string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
00982                 char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
00983                 int atom_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
00984                 char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
00985                 char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
00986                 stringstream sss;
00987                 sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << atom_sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
00988                 string key = sss.str();
00989                 if(target_key.compare(key) != 0)
00990                 {
00991                     serial_number_mapping_[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = serial_number;
00992                     atom->SetAtomSerialNumber(serial_number);
00993                     updated_atoms[serial_number] = atom;
00994                     serial_number++;
00995                 }
00996                 else
00997                 {
00998                     if(serial_number_mapping_.find(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()) != serial_number_mapping_.end())
00999                     {
01000                         serial_number_mapping_.erase(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber());
01001                     }
01002                 }
01003             }
01004             atom_card->SetAtoms(updated_atoms);
01005             updated_atom_cards.push_back(atom_card);
01006             serial_number++;
01007         }
01008         residue_set->SetAtoms(updated_atom_cards);
01009         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
01010         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector updated_heterogen_atom_cards = PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector();
01011         for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
01012         {
01013             PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
01014             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
01015             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap updated_heterogen_atoms;
01016             for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
01017             {
01018                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
01019                 string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
01020                 char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
01021                 int heterogen_atom_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
01022                 char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
01023                 char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
01024                 stringstream sss;
01025                 sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << heterogen_atom_sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
01026                 string key = sss.str();
01027                 if(target_key.compare(key) != 0)
01028                 {
01029                     serial_number_mapping_[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = serial_number;
01030                     atom->SetAtomSerialNumber(serial_number);
01031                     updated_heterogen_atoms[serial_number] = atom;
01032                     serial_number++;
01033                 }
01034                 else
01035                 {
01036                     if(serial_number_mapping_.find(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()) != serial_number_mapping_.end())
01037                     {
01038                         serial_number_mapping_.erase(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber());
01039                     }
01040                 }
01041             }
01042             heterogen_atom_card->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atoms);
01043             updated_heterogen_atom_cards.push_back(heterogen_atom_card);
01044         }
01045         residue_set->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atom_cards);
01046         
01047         model->SetModelResidueSet(residue_set);
01048         (*it).second = model;
01049     }
01050     models_->SetModels(models);
01051     this->UpdateConnectCard();
01052 }

01054 void PdbFile::DeleteResidues(PdbResidueVector target_residues)
01055 {
01056     map<string, PdbResidue* > pdb_residue_map = map<string, PdbResidue* >();
01057     for(PdbResidueVector::iterator it = target_residues.begin(); it != target_residues.end(); it++)
01058     {
01059         PdbResidue* residue = (*it);
01060         string target_residue_name = residue->GetResidueName();
01061         char target_residue_chain_id = residue->GetResidueChainId();
01062         int target_residue_sequence_number = residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
01063         char target_residue_insertion_code = residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
01064         char target_residue_alternate_location = residue->GetResidueAlternateLocation();

01066         ss << target_residue_name << "_" << target_residue_chain_id << "_" << target_residue_sequence_number << "_" << target_residue_insertion_code << "_" << target_residue_alternate_location;

01069     }

01080         {

01370 
01371 void PdbFile::DeleteAtom(PdbAtom* target_atom)
01372 {
01373     string target_residue_name = target_atom->GetAtomResidueName();
01374     char target_residue_chain_id = target_atom->GetAtomChainId();
01375     int target_residue_sequence_number = target_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
01376     char target_residue_insertion_code = target_atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
01377     char target_residue_alternate_location = target_atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
01378     stringstream ss;
01379     ss << target_residue_name << "_" << target_residue_chain_id << "_" << target_residue_sequence_number << "_" << target_residue_insertion_code << "_" << target_residue_alternate_location;
01380     string target_key = ss.str();
01381     
01382     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
01383     for(PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap::iterator it = models.begin();it != models.end(); it++)
01384     {
01385         PdbModel* model = (*it).second;
01386         PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
01387         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
01388         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector updated_atom_cards;
01389         int serial_number = 1;
01390         
01391         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
01392         {
01393             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
01394             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
01395             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap updated_atoms;
01396             
01397             for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
01398             {
01399                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
01400                 string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
01401                 char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
01402                 int sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
01403                 char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
01404                 char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
01405                 stringstream sss;
01406                 sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
01407                 string key = sss.str();
01408                 if(target_key.compare(key) != 0)
01409                 {
01410                     serial_number_mapping_[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = serial_number;
01411                     atom->SetAtomSerialNumber(serial_number);
01412                     updated_atoms[serial_number] = atom;
01413                     serial_number++;
01414                 }
01415                 else
01416                 {
01417                     string atom_name = atom->GetAtomName();
01418                     if(atom_name.compare(target_atom->GetAtomName()) != 0)
01419                     {
01420                         serial_number_mapping_[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = serial_number;
01421                         atom->SetAtomSerialNumber(serial_number);
01422                         updated_atoms[serial_number] = atom;
01423                         serial_number++;
01424                     }
01425                     else
01426                     {
01427                         if(serial_number_mapping_.find(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()) != serial_number_mapping_.end())
01428                         {
01429                             serial_number_mapping_.erase(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber());
01430                         }
01431                     }
01432                 }
01433             }
01434             atom_card->SetAtoms(updated_atoms);
01435             updated_atom_cards.push_back(atom_card);
01436             serial_number++;
01437         }
01438         residue_set->SetAtoms(updated_atom_cards);
01439         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
01440         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector updated_heterogen_atom_cards;
01441         for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
01442         {
01443             PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
01444             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
01445             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap updated_heterogen_atoms;
01446             for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
01447             {
01448                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
01449                 string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
01450                 char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
01451                 int sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
01452                 char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
01453                 char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
01454                 stringstream sss;
01455                 sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
01456                 string key = sss.str();
01457                 if(target_key.compare(key) != 0)
01458                 {
01459                     serial_number_mapping_[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = serial_number;
01460                     atom->SetAtomSerialNumber(serial_number);
01461                     updated_heterogen_atoms[serial_number] = atom;
01462                     serial_number++;
01463                 }
01464                 else
01465                 {
01466                     string atom_name = atom->GetAtomName();
01467                     if(atom_name.compare(target_atom->GetAtomName()) != 0)
01468                     {
01469                         serial_number_mapping_[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = serial_number;
01470                         atom->SetAtomSerialNumber(serial_number);
01471                         updated_heterogen_atoms[serial_number] = atom;
01472                         serial_number++;
01473                     }
01474                     else
01475                     {
01476                         if(serial_number_mapping_.find(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()) != serial_number_mapping_.end())
01477                         {
01478                             serial_number_mapping_.erase(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber());
01479                         }
01480                     }
01481                 }
01482             }
01483             heterogen_atom_card->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atoms);
01484             updated_heterogen_atom_cards.push_back(heterogen_atom_card);
01485         }
01486         residue_set->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atom_cards);
01487         
01488         model->SetModelResidueSet(residue_set);
01489         (*it).second = model;
01490     }
01491     models_->SetModels(models);
01492     this->UpdateConnectCard();
01493 }

01495 void PdbFile::DeleteAtoms(PdbAtomVector target_atoms)
01496 {
01497     map<string, PdbAtom* > pdb_atom_map = map<string, PdbAtom* >();
01498     for(PdbAtomVector::iterator it = target_atoms.begin(); it != target_atoms.end(); it++)
01499     {
01500         PdbAtom* target_atom = (*it);
01501         string target_residue_name = target_atom->GetAtomResidueName();
01502         char target_residue_chain_id = target_atom->GetAtomChainId();
01503         int target_residue_sequence_number = target_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
01504         char target_residue_insertion_code = target_atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
01505         char target_residue_alternate_location = target_atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
01506         stringstream ss;
01507         ss << target_residue_name << "_" << target_residue_chain_id << "_" << target_residue_sequence_number << "_" << target_residue_insertion_code << "_" << target_residue_alternate_location;
01508         string target_key = ss.str();
01509         pdb_atom_map[target_key] = target_atom;
01510     }
01511 
01512     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
01513     for(PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap::iterator it = models.begin();it != models.end(); it++)
01514     {
01515         PdbModel* model = (*it).second;

01517         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
01518         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector updated_atom_cards;
01519         int serial_number = 1;
01520 
01521         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
01522         {
01523             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);

01561                         }
01562                     }
01563                 }
01564             }

01567             serial_number++;

01882 
01883 void PdbFile::UpdateResidueName(PdbResidue *residue, string updated_residue_name)
01884 {
01885     string target_residue_name = residue->GetResidueName();
01886     char target_residue_chain_id = residue->GetResidueChainId();
01887     int target_residue_sequence_number = residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
01888     char target_residue_insertion_code = residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
01889     char target_residue_alternate_location = residue->GetResidueAlternateLocation();
01890     stringstream ss;
01891     ss << target_residue_name << "_" << target_residue_chain_id << "_" << target_residue_sequence_number << "_" << target_residue_insertion_code << "_" << target_residue_alternate_location;
01892     string target_key = ss.str();
01893     
01894     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
01895     for(PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap::iterator it = models.begin();it != models.end(); it++)
01896     {
01897         PdbModel* model = (*it).second;
01898         PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
01899         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
01900         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector updated_atom_cards;
01901         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
01902         {
01903             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
01904             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
01905             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap updated_atoms;
01906             
01907             for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
01908             {
01909                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
01910                 string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
01911                 char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
01912                 int atom_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
01913                 char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
01914                 char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
01915                 stringstream sss;
01916                 sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << atom_sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
01917                 string key = sss.str();
01918                 if(target_key.compare(key) == 0)
01919                 {
01920                     atom->SetAtomResidueName(updated_residue_name);
01921                     updated_atoms[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = atom;
01922                 }
01923                 else
01924                 {
01925                     updated_atoms[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = atom;
01926                 }
01927             }
01928             atom_card->SetAtoms(updated_atoms);
01929             updated_atom_cards.push_back(atom_card);
01930         }
01931         residue_set->SetAtoms(updated_atom_cards);
01932         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
01933         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector updated_heterogen_atom_cards;
01934         for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
01935         {
01936             PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
01937             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
01938             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap updated_heterogen_atoms;
01939             for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
01940             {
01941                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
01942                 string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
01943                 char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
01944                 int heterogen_atom_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
01945                 char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
01946                 char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
01947                 stringstream sss;
01948                 sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << heterogen_atom_sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
01949                 string key = sss.str();
01950                 if(target_key.compare(key) == 0)
01951                 {
01952                     atom->SetAtomResidueName(updated_residue_name);
01953                     updated_heterogen_atoms[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = atom;
01954                 }
01955                 else
01956                 {
01957                     updated_heterogen_atoms[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = atom;
01958                 }
01959             }
01960             heterogen_atom_card->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atoms);
01961             updated_heterogen_atom_cards.push_back(heterogen_atom_card);
01962         }
01963         residue_set->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atom_cards);
01964         
01965         model->SetModelResidueSet(residue_set);
01966         (*it).second = model;
01967     }
01968     models_->SetModels(models);
01969 }

01971 void PdbFile::UpdateResidueNameWithTheGivenModelNumber(PdbResidue *residue, string updated_residue_name, int model_number)
01972 {
01973     string target_residue_name = residue->GetResidueName();
01974     char target_residue_chain_id = residue->GetResidueChainId();
01975     int target_residue_sequence_number = residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
01976     char target_residue_insertion_code = residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
01977     char target_residue_alternate_location = residue->GetResidueAlternateLocation();
01978     stringstream ss;
01979     ss << target_residue_name << "_" << target_residue_chain_id << "_" << target_residue_sequence_number << "_" << target_residue_insertion_code << "_" << target_residue_alternate_location;
01980     string target_key = ss.str();
01981 
01982     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
01983     if(models.size() != 0)
01984     {
01985         PdbModel* model = models[model_number];
01986         PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
01987         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
01988         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector updated_atom_cards;
01989         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
01990         {
01991             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
01992             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
01993             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap updated_atoms;
01994 
01995             for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
01996             {

01999                 char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
02000                 int atom_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02001                 char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
02002                 char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
02003                 stringstream sss;
02004                 sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << atom_sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
02005                 string key = sss.str();
02006                 if(target_key.compare(key) == 0)
02007                 {
02008                     atom->SetAtomResidueName(updated_residue_name);
02009                     updated_atoms[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = atom;
02010                 }
02011                 else
02012                 {
02013                     updated_atoms[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = atom;
02014                 }
02015             }
02016             atom_card->SetAtoms(updated_atoms);
02017             updated_atom_cards.push_back(atom_card);
02018         }
02019         residue_set->SetAtoms(updated_atom_cards);
02020         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
02021         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector updated_heterogen_atom_cards;
02022         for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
02023         {
02024             PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
02025             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
02026             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap updated_heterogen_atoms;
02027             for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
02028             {
02029                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
02030                 string residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
02031                 char chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
02032                 int heterogen_atom_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02033                 char insertion_code = atom->GetAtomInsertionCode();
02034                 char alternate_location = atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation();
02035                 stringstream sss;
02036                 sss << residue_name << "_" << chain_id << "_" << heterogen_atom_sequence_number << "_" << insertion_code << "_" << alternate_location;
02037                 string key = sss.str();
02038                 if(target_key.compare(key) == 0)
02039                 {
02040                     atom->SetAtomResidueName(updated_residue_name);
02041                     updated_heterogen_atoms[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = atom;
02042                 }
02043                 else
02044                 {
02045                     updated_heterogen_atoms[atom->GetAtomSerialNumber()] = atom;
02046                 }
02047             }
02048             heterogen_atom_card->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atoms);
02049             updated_heterogen_atom_cards.push_back(heterogen_atom_card);
02050         }
02051         residue_set->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atom_cards);
02052

02060 void PdbFile::InsertResidueBefore(PdbAtomCard* residue)
02061 {
02062     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
02063     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap updated_models;
02064     for(PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap::iterator it = models.begin(); it != models.end(); it++)
02065     {
02066         PdbModel* model = (*it).second;
02067         PdbModel* updated_model = new PdbModel();
02068         updated_model->SetModelSerialNumber(model->GetModelSerialNumber());
02069         PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
02070         PdbModelResidueSet* updated_residue_set = new PdbModelResidueSet();
02071         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
02072         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector updated_atom_cards;
02073         int serial_number = 1;
02074         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
02075         {
02076             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
02077             PdbAtomCard* updated_atom_card = new PdbAtomCard();
02078             updated_atom_card->SetRecordName(atom_card->GetRecordName());
02079             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
02080             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap updated_atoms;
02081             int sequence_number = 1;
02082             bool located = true;
02083 
02084             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms_of_residue = residue->GetAtoms();
02085             PdbAtom* first_atom_in_residue = (*(atoms_of_residue.begin())).second;
02086             char residue_chain_id = first_atom_in_residue->GetAtomChainId();
02087             int residue_sequence_number = first_atom_in_residue->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02088 
02089             for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
02090             {
02091                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
02092 
02093                 if(residue_chain_id == atom->GetAtomChainId() && residue_sequence_number == atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02094                 {
02095                     if(it2 != atoms.begin())
02096                     {
02097                         PdbAtom* previous_atom = (*(--it2)).second;
02098                         it2++;
02099                         if(previous_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02100                         {
02101                             int diff = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() - previous_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02102                             if(diff == 1)
02103                                 sequence_number++;
02104                             else
02105                                 sequence_number += diff;
02106                         }
02107                     }
02108                     else
02109                         sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02110                     if(located)
02111                     {
02112                         for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it3 = atoms_of_residue.begin(); it3 != atoms_of_residue.end(); it3++)
02113                         {
02114                             PdbAtom* atom_of_residue = (*it3).second;
02115                             PdbAtom* new_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom_of_residue->GetAtomName(),atom_of_residue->GetAtomAlternateLocation(),
02116                                                             atom_of_residue->GetAtomResidueName(),atom_of_residue->GetAtomChainId(), sequence_number,
02117                                                             atom_of_residue->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom_of_residue->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02118                                                             atom_of_residue->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom_of_residue->GetAtomTempretureFactor(),
02119                                                             atom_of_residue->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom_of_residue->GetAtomCharge());
02120                             updated_atoms[serial_number] = new_atom;
02121                             serial_number++;
02122                         }
02123                         sequence_number_mapping_[sequence_number] = iNotSet;
02124                         sequence_number++;
02125                         located = false;
02126                     }
02127                     if(!located)
02128                     {
02129                         PdbAtom* updated_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom->GetAtomName(),atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(), atom->GetAtomResidueName(),
02130                                                             atom->GetAtomChainId(), sequence_number, atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02131                                                             atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(), atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom->GetAtomCharge());
02132                         updated_atoms[serial_number] = updated_atom;
02133                         serial_number++;
02134                         if(sequence_number != atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02135                             sequence_number_mapping_[sequence_number] = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02136                     }
02137                 }
02138                 else
02139                 {
02140                     if(it2 != atoms.begin())
02141                     {
02142 
02143                         PdbAtom* previous_atom = (*(--it2)).second;
02144                         it2++;
02145                         if(previous_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02146                         {
02147                             int diff = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() - previous_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02148                             if(diff == 1)
02149                                 sequence_number++;
02150                             else
02151                                 sequence_number += diff;
02152                         }
02153                     }
02154                     else
02155                         sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02156                     PdbAtom* updated_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom->GetAtomName(),atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(), atom->GetAtomResidueName(),
02157                                                         atom->GetAtomChainId(), sequence_number, atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02158                                                         atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(), atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom->GetAtomCharge());
02159                     updated_atoms[serial_number] = updated_atom;
02160                     serial_number++;
02161                     if(sequence_number != atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02162                         sequence_number_mapping_[sequence_number] = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02163                 }
02164             }
02165             updated_atom_card->SetAtoms(updated_atoms);
02166             updated_atom_cards.push_back(updated_atom_card);
02167             serial_number++;
02168         }
02169         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
02170         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector updated_heterogen_atom_cards;
02171         for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
02172         {
02173             PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
02174             PdbHeterogenAtomCard* updated_heterogen_atom_card = new PdbHeterogenAtomCard();
02175             updated_heterogen_atom_card->SetRecordName(heterogen_atom_card->GetRecordName());
02176             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
02177             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap updated_heterogen_atoms;
02178             for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
02179             {
02180                 PdbAtom* heterogen_atom = (*it2).second;
02181                 PdbAtom* updated_heterogen_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, heterogen_atom->GetAtomName(),heterogen_atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(),
02182                                                               heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueName(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomChainId(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber(),
02183                                                               heterogen_atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02184                                                               heterogen_atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(),
02185                                                               heterogen_atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomCharge());
02186                 updated_heterogen_atoms[serial_number] = updated_heterogen_atom;
02187                 serial_number++;
02188             }
02189             updated_heterogen_atom_card->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atoms);
02190             updated_heterogen_atom_cards.push_back(updated_heterogen_atom_card);
02191         }
02192         updated_residue_set->SetAtoms(updated_atom_cards);
02193         updated_residue_set->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atom_cards);
02194         updated_model->SetModelResidueSet(updated_residue_set);
02195         updated_models[updated_model->GetModelSerialNumber()] = updated_model;
02196     }
02197     models_->SetModels(updated_models);
02198 }

02341 void PdbFile::InsertResidueAfter(PdbAtomCard* residue)
02342 {
02343     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
02344     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap updated_models;
02345     for(PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap::iterator it = models.begin(); it != models.end(); it++)
02346     {
02347         PdbModel* model = (*it).second;
02348         PdbModel* updated_model = new PdbModel();
02349         updated_model->SetModelSerialNumber(model->GetModelSerialNumber());
02350         PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
02351         PdbModelResidueSet* updated_residue_set = new PdbModelResidueSet();
02352         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
02353         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector updated_atom_cards;
02354         int serial_number = 1;
02355         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
02356         {
02357             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
02358             PdbAtomCard* updated_atom_card = new PdbAtomCard();
02359             updated_atom_card->SetRecordName(atom_card->GetRecordName());
02360             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
02361             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap updated_atoms;
02362             int sequence_number = 1;
02363             bool located = false;
02364             
02365             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms_of_residue = residue->GetAtoms();
02366             PdbAtom* first_atom_in_residue = (*(atoms_of_residue.begin())).second;
02367             char residue_chain_id = first_atom_in_residue->GetAtomChainId();
02368             int residue_sequence_number = first_atom_in_residue->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02369             
02370             for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
02371             {
02372                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
02373                 
02374                 if(residue_chain_id == atom->GetAtomChainId() && residue_sequence_number == atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02375                 {
02376                     if(it2 != atoms.begin())
02377                     {
02378                         PdbAtom* previous_atom = (*(--it2)).second;
02379                         it2++;
02380                         if(previous_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02381                         {
02382                             int diff = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() - previous_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02383                             if(diff == 1)
02384                                 sequence_number++;
02385                             else
02386                                 sequence_number += diff;
02387                         }
02388                     }
02389                     else
02390                     {
02391                         sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02392                     }
02393                     PdbAtom* updated_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom->GetAtomName(),atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(), atom->GetAtomResidueName(),
02394                                                         atom->GetAtomChainId(), sequence_number, atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02395                                                         atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(), atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom->GetAtomCharge());
02396                     updated_atoms[serial_number] = updated_atom;
02397                     serial_number++;
02398                     if(sequence_number != atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02399                         sequence_number_mapping_[sequence_number] = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02400                     located = true;
02401                 }
02402                 else
02403                 {
02404                     if(located)
02405                     {
02406                         sequence_number++;
02407                         for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it3 = atoms_of_residue.begin(); it3 != atoms_of_residue.end(); it3++)
02408                         {
02409                             PdbAtom* atom_of_residue = (*it3).second;
02410                             PdbAtom* new_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom_of_residue->GetAtomName(),atom_of_residue->GetAtomAlternateLocation(),
02411                                                             atom_of_residue->GetAtomResidueName(),atom_of_residue->GetAtomChainId(), sequence_number,
02412                                                             atom_of_residue->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom_of_residue->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02413                                                             atom_of_residue->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom_of_residue->GetAtomTempretureFactor(),
02414                                                             atom_of_residue->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom_of_residue->GetAtomCharge());
02415                             updated_atoms[serial_number] = new_atom;
02416                             serial_number++;
02417                         }
02418                         sequence_number_mapping_[sequence_number] = iNotSet;
02419                         located = false;
02420                     }
02421                     if(!located)
02422                     {
02423                         if(it2 != atoms.begin())
02424                         {
02425                             PdbAtom* previous_atom = (*(--it2)).second;
02426                             it2++;
02427                             if(previous_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02428                             {
02429                                 int diff = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() - previous_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02430                                 if(diff == 1)
02431                                     sequence_number++;
02432                                 else
02433                                     sequence_number += diff;
02434                             }
02435                         }
02436                         else
02437                         {
02438                             sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02439                         }
02440                         PdbAtom* updated_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom->GetAtomName(),atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(), atom->GetAtomResidueName(),
02441                                                             atom->GetAtomChainId(), sequence_number, atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02442                                                             atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(), atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom->GetAtomCharge());
02443                         updated_atoms[serial_number] = updated_atom;
02444                         serial_number++;
02445                         if(sequence_number != atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber())
02446                             sequence_number_mapping_[sequence_number] = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02447                     }
02448                 }
02449                 if(it2 == --atoms.end() && located)
02450                 {
02451                     sequence_number++;
02452                     for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it3 = atoms_of_residue.begin(); it3 != atoms_of_residue.end(); it3++)
02453                     {
02454                         PdbAtom* atom_of_residue = (*it3).second;
02455                         PdbAtom* new_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom_of_residue->GetAtomName(),atom_of_residue->GetAtomAlternateLocation(),
02456                                                         atom_of_residue->GetAtomResidueName(),atom_of_residue->GetAtomChainId(), sequence_number,
02457                                                         atom_of_residue->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom_of_residue->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02458                                                         atom_of_residue->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom_of_residue->GetAtomTempretureFactor(),
02459                                                         atom_of_residue->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom_of_residue->GetAtomCharge());
02460                         updated_atoms[serial_number] = new_atom;
02461                         serial_number++;
02462                     }
02463                     sequence_number_mapping_[sequence_number] = iNotSet;
02464                     located = false;
02465                     sequence_number++;
02466                 }
02467             }
02468             updated_atom_card->SetAtoms(updated_atoms);
02469             updated_atom_cards.push_back(updated_atom_card);
02470             serial_number++;
02471         }
02472         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
02473         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector updated_heterogen_atom_cards;
02474         for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
02475         {
02476             PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
02477             PdbHeterogenAtomCard* updated_heterogen_atom_card = new PdbHeterogenAtomCard();
02478             updated_heterogen_atom_card->SetRecordName(heterogen_atom_card->GetRecordName());
02479             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
02480             PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap updated_heterogen_atoms;
02481             for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
02482             {
02483                 PdbAtom* heterogen_atom = (*it2).second;
02484                 PdbAtom* updated_heterogen_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, heterogen_atom->GetAtomName(),heterogen_atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(),
02485                                                               heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueName(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomChainId(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber(),
02486                                                               heterogen_atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02487                                                               heterogen_atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(),
02488                                                               heterogen_atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), heterogen_atom->GetAtomCharge());
02489                 updated_heterogen_atoms[serial_number] = updated_heterogen_atom;
02490                 serial_number++;
02491             }
02492             updated_heterogen_atom_card->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atoms);
02493             updated_heterogen_atom_cards.push_back(updated_heterogen_atom_card);
02494         }
02495         updated_residue_set->SetAtoms(updated_atom_cards);
02496         updated_residue_set->SetHeterogenAtoms(updated_heterogen_atom_cards);
02497         updated_model->SetModelResidueSet(updated_residue_set);
02498         updated_models[updated_model->GetModelSerialNumber()] = updated_model;
02499     }
02500     models_->SetModels(updated_models);
02501 }

02602                                                             atom->GetAtomChainId(), sequence_number, atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02603                                                             atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(), atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom->GetAtomCharge());
02604                         updated_atoms[serial_number] = updated_atom;
02605                         serial_number++;
