02663 void PdbFile::SplitAtomCardOfModelCard(char split_point_chain_id, int split_point_sequence_number)
02664 {
02665     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
02666     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap updated_models;
02667     for(PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap::iterator it = models.begin(); it != models.end(); it++)
02668     {
02669         PdbModel* model = (*it).second;
02670         PdbModel* updated_model = new PdbModel();
02671         updated_model->SetModelSerialNumber(model->GetModelSerialNumber());
02672         PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
02673         PdbModelResidueSet* updated_residue_set = new PdbModelResidueSet();
02674         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
02675         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector updated_atom_cards;
02676         int serial_number = 1;
02677         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
02678         {
02679             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
02680             PdbAtomCard* updated_atom_card_first_part = new PdbAtomCard();
02681             PdbAtomCard* updated_atom_card_second_part = new PdbAtomCard();
02682             updated_atom_card_first_part->SetRecordName(atom_card->GetRecordName());
02683             updated_atom_card_second_part->SetRecordName(atom_card->GetRecordName());
02684             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
02685             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms_first_part;
02686             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms_second_part;
02687             
02688             bool located = false;
02689             for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
02690             {
02691                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
02692                 char residue_chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
02693                 int residue_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02694                 
02695                 if(residue_chain_id == split_point_chain_id && residue_sequence_number == split_point_sequence_number)
02696                 {
02697                     located = true;
02698                 }
02699                 if(located)
02700                 {
02701                     serial_number++;
02702                     PdbAtom* updated_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom->GetAtomName(),atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(), atom->GetAtomResidueName(),
02703                                                         atom->GetAtomChainId(), atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber(), atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02704                                                         atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(), atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom->GetAtomCharge());
02705                     atoms_second_part[serial_number] = updated_atom;
02706                 }
02707                 if(!located)
02708                 {
02709                     PdbAtom* updated_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom->GetAtomName(),atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(), atom->GetAtomResidueName(),
02710                                                         atom->GetAtomChainId(), atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber(), atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02711                                                         atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(), atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom->GetAtomCharge());
02712                     atoms_first_part[serial_number] = updated_atom;
02713                     serial_number++;
02714                 }
02715             }
02716             updated_atom_card_first_part->SetAtoms(atoms_first_part);
02717             updated_atom_card_second_part->SetAtoms(atoms_second_part);
02718             if(atoms_first_part.size() > 0)
02719             {
02720                 updated_atom_cards.push_back(updated_atom_card_first_part);
02721                 serial_number++;
02722             }
02723             if(atoms_second_part.size() > 0)
02724             {
02725                 updated_atom_cards.push_back(updated_atom_card_second_part);
02726                 serial_number++;
02727             }
02728         }
02729         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
02730         
02731         updated_residue_set->SetAtoms(updated_atom_cards);
02732         updated_residue_set->SetHeterogenAtoms(heterogen_atom_cards);
02733         updated_model->SetModelResidueSet(updated_residue_set);
02734         updated_models[updated_model->GetModelSerialNumber()] = updated_model;
02735     }
02736     models_->SetModels(updated_models);
02737 }
02738 
02739 void PdbFile::SplitAtomCardOfModelCardWithTheGivenModelNumber(char split_point_chain_id, int split_point_sequence_number, int model_number)
02740 {
02741     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
02742     if(models.size() != 0)
02743     {
02744         PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap updated_models;
02745         PdbModel* model = models[model_number];
02746         PdbModel* updated_model = new PdbModel();
02747         updated_model->SetModelSerialNumber(model->GetModelSerialNumber());
02748         PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
02749         PdbModelResidueSet* updated_residue_set = new PdbModelResidueSet();
02750         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
02751         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector updated_atom_cards;
02752         int serial_number = 1;
02753         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
02754         {
02755             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
02756             PdbAtomCard* updated_atom_card_first_part = new PdbAtomCard();
02757             PdbAtomCard* updated_atom_card_second_part = new PdbAtomCard();
02758             updated_atom_card_first_part->SetRecordName(atom_card->GetRecordName());
02759             updated_atom_card_second_part->SetRecordName(atom_card->GetRecordName());
02760             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
02761             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms_first_part;
02762             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms_second_part;
02763 
02764             bool located = false;
02765             for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
02766             {
02767                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
02768                 char residue_chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
02769                 int residue_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
02770 
02771                 if(residue_chain_id == split_point_chain_id && residue_sequence_number == split_point_sequence_number)
02772                 {
02773                     located = true;
02774                 }
02775                 if(located)
02776                 {
02777                     serial_number++;
02778                     PdbAtom* updated_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom->GetAtomName(),atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(), atom->GetAtomResidueName(),
02779                                                         atom->GetAtomChainId(), atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber(), atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02780                                                         atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(), atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom->GetAtomCharge());
02781                     atoms_second_part[serial_number] = updated_atom;
02782                 }
02783                 if(!located)
02784                 {
02785                     PdbAtom* updated_atom = new PdbAtom(serial_number, atom->GetAtomName(),atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation(), atom->GetAtomResidueName(),
02786                                                         atom->GetAtomChainId(), atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber(), atom->GetAtomInsertionCode(), atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate(),
02787                                                         atom->GetAtomOccupancy(), atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor(), atom->GetAtomElementSymbol(), atom->GetAtomCharge());
02788                     atoms_first_part[serial_number] = updated_atom;
02789                     serial_number++;
02790                 }
02791             }
02792             updated_atom_card_first_part->SetAtoms(atoms_first_part);
02793             updated_atom_card_second_part->SetAtoms(atoms_second_part);
02794             if(atoms_first_part.size() > 0)
02795             {
02796                 updated_atom_cards.push_back(updated_atom_card_first_part);
02797                 serial_number++;
02798             }
02799             if(atoms_second_part.size() > 0)
02800             {
02801                 updated_atom_cards.push_back(updated_atom_card_second_part);
02802                 serial_number++;
02803             }
02804         }
02805         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
02806 
02807         updated_residue_set->SetAtoms(updated_atom_cards);
02808         updated_residue_set->SetHeterogenAtoms(heterogen_atom_cards);
02809         updated_model->SetModelResidueSet(updated_residue_set);
02810         updated_models[updated_model->GetModelSerialNumber()] = updated_model;
02811         models_->SetModels(updated_models);
02812     }
02813 }
02814 
02815 void PdbFile::UpdateConnectCard()
02816 {
02817     if(connectivities_ != NULL)
02818     {
02819         PdbConnectCard::BondedAtomsSerialNumbersMap bondedAtomsSerialNumbersMap = connectivities_->GetBondedAtomsSerialNumbers();
02820         PdbConnectCard::BondedAtomsSerialNumbersMap new_bonded_atoms_serial_numbers_map = PdbConnectCard::BondedAtomsSerialNumbersMap();
02821         for(PdbConnectCard::BondedAtomsSerialNumbersMap::iterator it = bondedAtomsSerialNumbersMap.begin(); it != bondedAtomsSerialNumbersMap.end(); it++)
02822         {
02823             int source_serial_number = (*it).first;
02824             vector<int> bonded_serial_numbers = (*it).second;
02825             if(serial_number_mapping_.find(source_serial_number) != serial_number_mapping_.end())
02826             {
02827                 int new_source_serial_number = serial_number_mapping_[source_serial_number];
02828                 new_bonded_atoms_serial_numbers_map[new_source_serial_number] = vector<int>();
02829                 for(vector<int>::iterator it1 = bonded_serial_numbers.begin(); it1 != bonded_serial_numbers.end(); it1++)
02830                 {
02831                     int bonded_serial_number = (*it1);
02832                     if(serial_number_mapping_.find(bonded_serial_number) != serial_number_mapping_.end())
02833                     {
02834                         int new_bonded_serial_number = serial_number_mapping_[bonded_serial_number];
02835                         new_bonded_atoms_serial_numbers_map[new_source_serial_number].push_back(new_bonded_serial_number);
02836                     }
02837                 }
02838             }
02839         }
02840         connectivities_->SetBondedAtomsSerialNumbers(new_bonded_atoms_serial_numbers_map);
02841     }
02842 }

02847 bool PdbFile::Read(ifstream &in_file)
02848 {
02849     if(!this->ParseCards(in_file))
02850         return false;
02851 }
02852 
02853 bool PdbFile::ParseCards(ifstream &in_stream)
02854 {
02855     string line;
02856     
02857     /// Unable to read file
02858     if (!getline(in_stream, line))
02859     {
02860         cout << "Wrong input file format" << endl;
02861         throw PdbFileProcessingException("Error reading file");
02862     }
02863     
02864     line = ExpandLine(line, iPdbLineLength);
02865     string record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02866     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02867     if(record_name.compare("HEADER") == 0)
02868     {
02869         if(!ParseHeaderCard(in_stream, line))
02870             return false;
02871     }
02872     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02873     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02874     if(record_name.compare("OBSLTE") == 0)
02875     {
02876         if(!ParseObsoleteCard(in_stream, line))
02877             return false;
02878     }
02879     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02880     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02881     if(record_name.compare("TITLE") == 0)
02882     {
02883         if(!ParseTitleCard(in_stream, line))
02884             return false;
02885     }
02886     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02887     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02888     if(record_name.compare("SPLIT") == 0)
02889     {
02890         if(!ParseSplitCard(in_stream, line))
02891             return false;
02892     }
02893     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02894     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02895     if(record_name.compare("CAVEAT") == 0)
02896     {
02897         if(!ParseCaveatCard(in_stream, line))
02898             return false;
02899     }
02900     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02901     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02902     if(record_name.compare("COMPND") == 0)
02903     {
02904         if(!ParseCompoundCard(in_stream, line))
02905             return false;
02906     }
02907     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02908     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02909     if(record_name.compare("SOURCE") == 0)
02910     {
02911         if(!ParseSourceCard(in_stream, line))
02912             return false;
02913     }
02914     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02915     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02916     if(record_name.compare("KEYWDS") == 0)
02917     {
02918         if(!ParseKeywordCard(in_stream, line))
02919                 return false;
02920     }
02921     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02922     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02923     if(record_name.compare("EXPDTA") == 0)
02924     {
02925         if(!ParseExpirationDateCard(in_stream, line))
02926             return false;
02927     }
02928     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02929     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02930     if(record_name.compare("NUMMDL") == 0)
02931     {
02932         if(!ParseNumModelCard(in_stream, line))
02933             return false;
02934     }
02935     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02936     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02937     if(record_name.compare("MDLTYP") == 0)
02938     {
02939         if(!ParseModelTypeCard(in_stream, line))
02940             return false;
02941     }
02942     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02943     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02944     if(record_name.compare("AUTHOR") == 0)
02945     {
02946         if(!ParseAuthorCard(in_stream, line))
02947             return false;
02948     }
02949     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02950     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02951     if(record_name.compare("REVDAT") == 0)
02952     {
02953         if(!ParseRevisionDateCard(in_stream, line))
02954             return false;
02955     }
02956     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02957     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02958     if(record_name.compare("SPRSDE") == 0)
02959     {
02960         if(!ParseSupersededEntriesCard(in_stream, line))
02961             return false;
02962     }
02963     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02964     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02965     if(record_name.compare("JRNL") == 0)
02966     {
02967         if(!ParseJournalCard(in_stream, line))
02968             return false;
02969     }
02970     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02971     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02972     if(record_name.compare("REMARK") == 0)
02973     {
02974         if(!ParseRemarkCard(in_stream, line))
02975             return false;
02976     }
02977     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02978     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02979     if(record_name.find("DBREF") != string::npos)
02980     {
02981         if(!ParseDatabaseReferenceCard(in_stream, line))
02982             return false;
02983     }
02984     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02985     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02986     if(record_name.compare("SEQADV") == 0)
02987     {
02988         if(!ParseSequenceAdvancedCard(in_stream, line))
02989             return false;
02990     }
02991     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02992     record_name = Trim(record_name);
02993     if(record_name.compare("SEQRES") == 0)
02994     {
02995         if(!ParseSequenceResidueCard(in_stream, line))
02996             return false;
02997     }
02998     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
02999     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03000     if(record_name.compare("MODRES") == 0)
03001     {
03002         if(!ParseModificationResidueCard(in_stream, line))
03003             return false;
03004     }
03005     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03006     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03007     if(record_name.compare("HET") == 0)
03008     {
03009         if(!ParseHeterogenCard(in_stream, line))
03010             return false;
03011     }
03012     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03013     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03014     if(record_name.compare("HETNAM") == 0)
03015     {
03016         if(!ParseHeterogenNameCard(in_stream, line))
03017             return false;
03018     }
03019     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03020     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03021     if(record_name.compare("HETSYN") == 0)
03022     {
03023         if(!ParseHeterogenSynonymCard(in_stream, line))
03024             return false;
03025     }
03026     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03027     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03028     if(record_name.compare("FORMUL") == 0)
03029     {
03030         if(!ParseFormulaCard(in_stream, line))
03031             return false;
03032     }
03033     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03034     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03035     if(record_name.compare("HELIX") == 0)
03036     {
03037         if(!ParseHelixCard(in_stream, line))
03038             return false;
03039     }
03040     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03041     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03042     if(record_name.compare("SHEET") == 0)
03043     {
03044         if(!ParseSheetCard(in_stream, line))
03045             return false;
03046     }
03047     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03048     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03049     if(record_name.compare("SSBOND") == 0)
03050     {
03051         if(!ParseDisulfideBondCard(in_stream, line))
03052             return false;
03053     }
03054     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03055     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03056     if(record_name.compare("LINK") == 0)
03057     {
03058         if(!ParseLinkCard(in_stream, line))
03059             return false;
03060     }
03061     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03062     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03063     if(record_name.compare("CISPEP") == 0)
03064     {
03065         if(!ParseCISPeptideCard(in_stream, line))
03066             return false;
03067     }
03068     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03069     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03070     if(record_name.compare("SITE") == 0)
03071     {
03072         if(!ParseSiteCard(in_stream, line))
03073            return false;
03074     }
03075     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03076     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03077     if(record_name.compare("CRYST1") == 0)
03078     {
03079         if(!ParseCrystallographyCard(in_stream, line))
03080             return false;
03081     }
03082     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03083     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03084     if(record_name.find("ORIGX") != string::npos)
03085     {
03086         if(!ParseOriginCard(in_stream, line))
03087             return false;
03088     }
03089     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03090     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03091     if(record_name.find("SCALE") != string::npos)
03092     {
03093         if(!ParseScaleCard(in_stream, line))
03094             return false;
03095     }
03096     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03097     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03098     if(record_name.find("MTRIX") != string::npos)
03099     {
03100         if(!ParseMatrixCard(in_stream, line))
03101             return false;
03102     }
03103     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03104     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03105     if(record_name.compare("MODEL") == 0 || record_name.compare("ATOM") == 0 || record_name.compare("HETATM") == 0)
03106     {
03107         if(!ParseModelCard(in_stream, line))
03108             return false;
03109     }
03110     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03111     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03112     if(record_name.compare("CONECT") == 0)
03113     {
03114         if(!ParseConnectivityCard(in_stream, line))
03115             return false;
03116     }
03117     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03118     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03119 
03120     if(record_name.compare("MODEL") == 0)
03121     {
03122         cout << "Multiple connect card between model cards --> Unexpected entry"  << endl;
03123         return false;
03124     }
03125     if(record_name.compare("MASTER") == 0)
03126     {
03127         if(!ParseMasterCard(in_stream, line))
03128             return false;
03129     }
03130     record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03131     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03132     if(record_name.find("END") != string::npos || record_name.compare("END") == 0)
03133     {
03134         if(!ParseEndCard(in_stream, line))
03135             return false;
03136         return true;
03137     }
03138     else
03139     {
03140         cout << "Wrong input file format" << endl;
03141         return false;
03142     }
03143     return true;
03144 }
03145 
03146 bool PdbFile::ParseHeaderCard(std::ifstream& stream, string& line)
03147 {
03148     stringstream stream_block;
03149     stream_block << line << endl;
03150     if(!getline(stream, line))
03151     {
03152         cout << "Header card corupption" << endl;
03153         cout << "Wrong input file format" << endl;
03154         return false;
03155     }
03156     line = ExpandLine(line, iPdbLineLength);
03157     string record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03158     record_name = Trim(record_name);
03159     
03160     while(record_name.compare("HEADER") == 0)
03161     {
03162         stream_block << line << endl;
03163         if(getline(stream, line))
03164         {
03165             line = ExpandLine(line, iPdbLineLength);
03166             record_name = line.substr(0,6);
03167             record_name = Trim(record_name);
03168         }
03169         else
03170         {
03171             cout << "Header card corruption" << endl;
03172             cout << "Wrong input file format" << endl;
03173             return false;
03174         }
03175     }
03176     
03177     header_ = new PdbHeaderCard(stream_block);
03178     return true;
03179 }

03382 
03383 bool PdbFile::ParseKeywordCard(std::ifstream& stream, string& line)
03384 {
03385     stringstream stream_block;
03386     stream_block << line << endl;

04089         {
04090             cout << "Link card corruption" << endl;
04091             cout << "Wrong input file format" << endl;
04092             return false;
04093         }
04094     }
04095     
04096     links_ = new PdbLinkCard(stream_block);
04097     return true;
04098 }
04099 
04100 bool PdbFile::ParseCISPeptideCard(std::ifstream& stream, string& line)
04101 {
04102     stringstream stream_block;
04103     stream_block << line << endl;
04104     if(!getline(stream, line))
04105     {
04106         cout << "CIS peptide card corruption" << endl;
04107         cout << "Wrong input file format" << endl;
04108         return false;
04109     }
04110     line = ExpandLine(line, iPdbLineLength);
04111     string record_name = line.substr(0,6);
04112     record_name = Trim(record_name);
04113     
04114     while(record_name.compare("CISPEP") == 0)
04115     {
04116         stream_block << line << endl;
04117         if(getline(stream, line))
04118         {
04119             line = ExpandLine(line, iPdbLineLength);
04120             record_name = line.substr(0,6);
04121             record_name = Trim(record_name);
04122         }
04123         else
04124         {
04125             cout << "CIS peptide card corruption" << endl;
04126             cout << "Wrong input file format" << endl;
04127             return false;
04128         }
04129     }
04130     return true;
04131 }

04308 bool PdbFile::ParseModelCard(std::ifstream& stream, string& line)
04309 {
04310     stringstream stream_block;
04311     stream_block << line << endl;
04312     if(!getline(stream, line))
04313     {
04314         cout << "Model card corruption" << endl;
04315         cout << "Wrong input file format" << endl;
04316         return false;
04317     }
04318     line = ExpandLine(line, iPdbLineLength);
04319     string record_name = line.substr(0,6);
04320     record_name = Trim(record_name);
04321 
04322     while(record_name.compare("MODEL") == 0 || record_name.compare("ATOM") == 0 || record_name.compare("ANISOU") == 0
04323           || record_name.compare("TER") == 0 || record_name.compare("HETATM") == 0 || record_name.compare("ENDMDL") == 0)
04324 //          || record_name.find("TER") != string::npos || record_name.find("ENDMDL") != string::npos)
04325     {
04326         stream_block << line << endl;
04327         if(getline(stream, line))
04328         {
04329             line = ExpandLine(line, iPdbLineLength);
04330             record_name = line.substr(0,6);
04331             record_name = Trim(record_name);
04332         }
04333         else
04334         {
04335             cout << "Model card corruption" << endl;
04336             cout << "Wrong input file format" << endl;
04337             return false;
04338         }
04339     }
04340     
04341     // Model card
04342     models_ = new PdbModelCard(stream_block);
04343     return true;
04344 }

04414 bool PdbFile::ParseEndCard(std::ifstream& stream, string& line)
04415 {
04416     stringstream stream_block;
04417     stream_block << line << endl;
04418     if(!getline(stream, line))
04419     {
04420         cout << "End of file" << endl;
04421         return true;
04422     }
04423 
04424     line = ExpandLine(line, iPdbLineLength);
04425     string record_name = line.substr(0,6);
04426     record_name = Trim(record_name);
04427     while(record_name.find("END") != string::npos || record_name.compare("END") == 0)
04428     {
04429         stream_block << line << endl;
04430         if(getline(stream, line))
04431         {
04432             line = ExpandLine(line, iPdbLineLength);
04433             record_name = line.substr(0,6);
04434             record_name = Trim(record_name);
04435         }
04436         else
04437         {
04438             cout << "End of file" << endl;
04439             return true;
04440         }
04441     }
04442     return true;
04443 }
04444 
04445 void PdbFile::Write(const std::string& pdb_file)
04446 {
04447     std::ofstream out_file;
04448     try
04449     {
04450         out_file.open(pdb_file.c_str());
04451     }
04452     catch(...)
04453     {
04454         throw PdbFileProcessingException(__LINE__,"File could not be created");
04455     }
04456     try
04457     {
04458         this->ResolveCards(out_file);
04459     }
04460     catch(...)
04461     {
04462         out_file.close();            /// Close the parameter files
04463     }
04464 }
04465 
04466 void PdbFile::WriteWithTheGivenModelNumber(const std::string& pdb_file, int model_number)
04467 {
04468     std::ofstream out_file;
04469     try
04470     {
04471         out_file.open(pdb_file.c_str());
04472     }
04473     catch(...)
04474     {
04475         throw PdbFileProcessingException(__LINE__,"File could not be created");
04476     }
04477     try
04478     {
04479         this->ResolveCardsWithTheGivenModelNumber(out_file, model_number);
04480     }
04481     catch(...)
04482     {
04483         out_file.close();            /// Close the parameter files
04484     }
04485 }

04487 void PdbFile::ResolveCards(std::ofstream& out_stream)
04488 {
04489     if(this->header_ != NULL)
04490     {
04491         this->ResolveHeaderCard(out_stream);
04492     }
04493     if(this->title_ != NULL)
04494     {
04495         this->ResolveTitleCard(out_stream);
04496     }
04497     if(this->compound_ != NULL)
04498     {
04499         this->ResolveCompoundCard(out_stream);
04500     }
04501     if(this->number_of_models_ != NULL)
04502     {
04503         this->ResolveCompoundCard(out_stream);
04504     }
04505     if(this->model_type_ != NULL)
04506     {
04507         this->ResolveNumModelCard(out_stream);
04508     }
04509     if(this->residues_sequence_ != NULL)
04510     {
04511         this->ResolveSequenceResidueCard(out_stream);
04512     }
04513     if(this->residue_modification_ != NULL)
04514     {
04515         this->ResolveModificationResidueCard(out_stream);
04516     }
04517     if(this->heterogens_ != NULL)
04518     {
04519         this->ResolveHeterogenCard(out_stream);
04520     }
04521     if(this->heterogens_name_ != NULL)
04522     {
04523         this->ResolveHeterogenNameCard(out_stream);
04524     }
04525     if(this->heterogen_synonyms_ != NULL)
04526     {
04527         this->ResolveHeterogenSynonymCard(out_stream);
04528     }
04529     if(this->formulas_ != NULL)
04530     {
04531         this->ResolveFormulaCard(out_stream);
04532     }
04533     if(this->helixes_ != NULL)
04534     {
04535         this->ResolveHelixCard(out_stream);
04536     }
04537     if(this->sheets_ != NULL)
04538     {
04539         this->ResolveSheetCard(out_stream);
04540     }
04541     if(this->disulfide_bonds_ != NULL)
04542     {
04543         this->ResolveDisulfideBondCard(out_stream);
04544     }
04545     if(this->links_ != NULL)
04546     {
04547         this->ResolveLinkCard(out_stream);
04548     }
04549     if(this->sites_ != NULL)
04550     {
04551         this->ResolveSiteCard(out_stream);
04552     }
04553     if(this->crystallography_ != NULL)
04554     {
04555         this->ResolveCrystallographyCard(out_stream);
04556     }
04557     if(this->origins_ != NULL)
04558     {
04559         this->ResolveOriginCard(out_stream);
04560     }
04561     if(this->scales_ != NULL)
04562     {
04563         this->ResolveScaleCard(out_stream);
04564     }
04565     if(this->matrices_ != NULL)
04566     {
04567         this->ResolveMatrixCard(out_stream);
04568     }
04569     if(this->models_ != NULL)
04570     {
04571         this->ResolveModelCard(out_stream);
04572     }
04573     if(this->connectivities_ != NULL)
04574     {
04575         this->ResolveConnectivityCard(out_stream);
04576     }
04577     this->ResolveEndCard(out_stream);
04578 }

04597     }
04598     if(this->model_type_ != NULL)
04599     {
04600         this->ResolveNumModelCard(out_stream);
04601     }
04602     if(this->residues_sequence_ != NULL)
04603     {
04604         this->ResolveSequenceResidueCard(out_stream);
04605     }
04606     if(this->residue_modification_ != NULL)
04607     {
04608         this->ResolveModificationResidueCard(out_stream);
04609     }
04610     if(this->heterogens_ != NULL)
04611     {
04612         this->ResolveHeterogenCard(out_stream);
04613     }
04614     if(this->heterogens_name_ != NULL)
04615     {
04616         this->ResolveHeterogenNameCard(out_stream);
04617     }
04618     if(this->heterogen_synonyms_ != NULL)
04619     {

04621     }

04623     {
04624         this->ResolveFormulaCard(out_stream);
04625     }

04627     {
04628         this->ResolveHelixCard(out_stream);
04629     }
04630     if(this->sheets_ != NULL)
04631     {
04632         this->ResolveSheetCard(out_stream);
04633     }
04634     if(this->disulfide_bonds_ != NULL)
04635     {
04636         this->ResolveDisulfideBondCard(out_stream);
04637     }
04638     if(this->links_ != NULL)
04639     {
04640         this->ResolveLinkCard(out_stream);
04641     }
04642     if(this->sites_ != NULL)
04643     {
04644         this->ResolveSiteCard(out_stream);
04645     }
04646     if(this->crystallography_ != NULL)
04647     {
04648         this->ResolveCrystallographyCard(out_stream);
04649     }
04650     if(this->origins_ != NULL)
04651     {
04652         this->ResolveOriginCard(out_stream);
04653     }

04655     {

04657     }

04665     }
04666     if(this->connectivities_ != NULL)
04667     {
04668         this->ResolveConnectivityCard(out_stream);
04669     }
04670     this->ResolveEndCard(out_stream);
04671 }
04672 
04673 void PdbFile::ResolveHeaderCard(std::ofstream& stream)
04674 {
04675     stream << left << setw(6) << header_->GetRecordName()
04676            << left << setw(4) << " "
04677            << left << setw(40) << header_->GetClassification()
04678            << left << setw(9) << header_->GetDepositionDate()
04679            << left << setw(3) << " "
04680            << right << setw(4) << header_->GetIdentifierCode()
04681            << left << setw(14) << " "
04682            << endl;
04683 }
04684 
04685 void PdbFile::ResolveObsoleteCard(std::ofstream& stream)
04686 {
04687 }
04688 
04689 void PdbFile::ResolveTitleCard(std::ofstream& stream)
04690 {
04691     const int MAX_TITLE_LENGTH_IN_LINE = 70;
04692     stream << left << setw(6) << title_->GetRecordName()
04693            << left << setw(2) << " ";
04694     if((int)title_->GetTitle().length() > MAX_TITLE_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
04695     {
04696         stream << right << setw(2) << " "
04697                << left << setw(70) << title_->GetTitle().substr(0,MAX_TITLE_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
04698                << endl;
04699         
04700         int counter = ceil((double)(title_->GetTitle().length()) / MAX_TITLE_LENGTH_IN_LINE);
04701         for(int i = 2; i <= counter; i++)
04702         {
04703             if(i != counter)
04704             {
04705                 stream << left << setw(6) << title_->GetRecordName()
04706                        << left << setw(2) << " "
04707                        << right << setw(2) << i
04708                        << left << setw(70) << title_->GetTitle().substr(MAX_TITLE_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1), MAX_TITLE_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
04709                        << endl;
04710             }
04711             else
04712             {
04713                 stream << left << setw(6) << title_->GetRecordName()
04714                        << left << setw(2) << " "
04715                        << right << setw(2) << i
04716                        << left << setw(70) << title_->GetTitle().substr(MAX_TITLE_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1), title_->GetTitle().length()-MAX_TITLE_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1))
04717                        << endl;
04718             }
04719         }
04720     }
04721     else
04722     {
04723         stream << right << setw(2) << " "
04724                << left << setw(70) << title_->GetTitle()
04725                << endl;
04726     }
04727 }

04738 
04739 void PdbFile::ResolveCompoundCard(std::ofstream& stream)
04740 {
04741     const int MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE = 70;
04742     stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04743            << left << setw(1) << " "
04744            << right << setw(3) << " ";
04745     
04746     PdbCompoundCard::PdbCompoundSpecificationMap compound_specification_map = compound_->GetCompoundSpecifications();
04747     if((*(compound_specification_map.begin())).second->GetMoleculeId() != "")
04748     {
04749         stringstream ss;
04750         ss << "MOL_ID: " << (*(compound_specification_map.begin())).second->GetMoleculeId() << ";";
04751         stream << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04752     }
04753     else
04754     {
04755         stringstream ss;
04756         ss << " UNKNOWN;";
04757         stream << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04758     }
04759     bool first = true;
04760     int counter = 2;
04761     for(PdbCompoundCard::PdbCompoundSpecificationMap::iterator it = compound_specification_map.begin(); it != compound_specification_map.end(); it++)
04762     {
04763         PdbCompoundSpecification* compound_specification = (*it).second;
04764         if(!first)
04765         {
04766             if(compound_specification->GetMoleculeId() != "")
04767             {
04768                 stringstream ss;
04769                 ss << " MOL_ID: " << compound_specification->GetMoleculeId() << ";";
04770                 stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04771                        << left << setw(1) << " "
04772                        << right << setw(3) << counter
04773                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04774                 counter++;
04775             }
04776             else
04777             {
04778                 stringstream ss;
04779                 ss << " UNKNOWN;";
04780                 stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04781                        << left << setw(1) << " "
04782                        << right << setw(3) << counter
04783                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04784                 counter++;
04785             }
04786         }
04787         
04788         /// Molecule name specification
04789         if(compound_specification->GetMoleculeName() != "")
04790         {
04791             stringstream molecule_name;
04792             molecule_name << " MOLECULE: " << compound_specification->GetMoleculeName() << ";";
04793             int length = molecule_name.str().length();
04794             
04795             if(length <= MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE)
04796             {
04797                 stringstream ss;
04798                 ss << molecule_name.str();
04799                 stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04800                        << left << setw(1) << " "
04801                        << right << setw(3) << counter
04802                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04803                 counter++;
04804             }
04805             else
04806             {
04807                 int number_of_lines = ceil((double)(length) / MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04808                 
04809                 for(int i = 1; i <= number_of_lines; i++)
04810                 {
04811                     if(i != number_of_lines)
04812                     {
04813                         stringstream ss;
04814                         ss << molecule_name.str().substr((i-1)*(MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE), MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04815                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04816                                << left << setw(1) << " "
04817                                << right << setw(3) << counter
04818                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str()
04819                                << endl;
04820                         counter++;
04821                     }
04822                     else
04823                     {
04824                         stringstream ss;
04825                         ss << molecule_name.str().substr((i-1)*(MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE), length - (i-1)*(MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE));
04826                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04827                                << left << setw(1) << " "
04828                                << right << setw(3) << counter
04829                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str()
04830                                << endl;
04831                         counter++;
04832                     }
04833                 }
04834                 
04835             }
04836         }
04837         
04838         /// Molecule chain ids specification
04839         if(compound_specification->GetChainIds().size() > 0)
04840         {
04841             vector<string> chain_ids = compound_specification->GetChainIds();
04842             stringstream chain_id;
04843             chain_id << " CHAIN: ";
04844             for(vector<string>::iterator it1 = chain_ids.begin(); it1 != chain_ids.end(); it1++)
04845             {
04846                 if(it1 < chain_ids.end()-1)
04847                     chain_id << (*it1) << ",";
04848                 else
04849                     chain_id << (*it1);
04850             }
04851             chain_id << ";";
04852             int length = chain_id.str().length();
04853             if(length <= MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE)
04854             {
04855                 stringstream ss;
04856                 ss << chain_id.str();
04857                 stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04858                        << left << setw(1) << " "
04859                        << right << setw(3) << counter
04860                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04861                 counter++;
04862             }
04863             else
04864             {
04865                 int number_of_lines = ceil((double)(length) / MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04866                 for(int i = 1; i <= number_of_lines; i++)
04867                 {
04868                     if(i != number_of_lines)
04869                     {
04870                         stringstream ss;
04871                         ss << chain_id.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04872                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04873                                << left << setw(1) << " "
04874                                << right << setw(3) << counter
04875                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04876                         counter++;
04877                     }
04878                     else
04879                     {
04880                         stringstream ss;
04881                         ss << chain_id.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, length - (i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04882                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04883                                << left << setw(1) << " "
04884                                << right << setw(3) << counter
04885                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04886                         counter++;
04887                     }
04888                 }
04889             }
04890         }
04891         
04892         /// Fragment specification
04893         if(compound_specification->GetFragment() != "")
04894         {
04895             stringstream fragment;
04896             fragment << " FRAGMENT: " << compound_specification->GetFragment() << ";";
04897             int length = fragment.str().length();
04898             if(length <= MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE)
04899             {
04900                 stringstream ss;
04901                 ss << ss.str();
04902                 stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04903                        << left << setw(1) << " "
04904                        << right << setw(3) << counter
04905                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04906                 counter++;
04907             }
04908             else
04909             {
04910                 int number_of_lines = ceil((double)(length) / MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04911                 for(int i = 1; i <= number_of_lines; i++)
04912                 {
04913                     if(i != number_of_lines)
04914                     {
04915                         stringstream ss;
04916                         ss << ss.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04917                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04918                                << left << setw(1) << " "
04919                                << right << setw(3) << counter
04920                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04921                         counter++;
04922                     }
04923                     else
04924                     {
04925                         stringstream ss;
04926                         ss << ss.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, length - (i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04927                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04928                                << left << setw(1) << " "
04929                                << right << setw(3) << counter
04930                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04931                         counter++;
04932                     }
04933                 }
04934             }
04935         }
04936         
04937         /// Molecule synonyms specification
04938         if(compound_specification->GetMoleculeSynonyms().size() > 0)
04939         {
04940             vector<string> molecule_synonyms = compound_specification->GetMoleculeSynonyms();
04941             stringstream synonyms;
04942             synonyms << " SYNONYM: ";
04943             for(vector<string>::iterator it1 = molecule_synonyms.begin(); it1 != molecule_synonyms.end(); it1++)
04944             {
04945                 if(it1 < molecule_synonyms.end()-1)
04946                     synonyms << (*it1) << ",";
04947                 else
04948                     synonyms << (*it1);
04949             }
04950             synonyms << ";";
04951             int length = synonyms.str().length();
04952             if(length <= MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE)
04953             {
04954                 stringstream ss;
04955                 ss << synonyms.str();
04956                 stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04957                        << left << setw(1) << " "
04958                        << right << setw(3) << counter
04959                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04960                 counter++;
04961             }
04962             else
04963             {
04964                 int number_of_lines = ceil((double)(length) / MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04965                 for(int i = 1; i <= number_of_lines; i++)
04966                 {
04967                     if(i != number_of_lines)
04968                     {
04969                         stringstream ss;
04970                         ss << synonyms.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04971                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04972                                << left << setw(1) << " "
04973                                << right << setw(3) << counter
04974                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04975                         counter++;
04976                     }
04977                     else
04978                     {
04979                         stringstream ss;
04980                         ss << synonyms.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, length - (i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
04981                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
04982                                << left << setw(1) << " "
04983                                << right << setw(3) << counter
04984                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
04985                         counter++;
04986                     }
04987                 }
04988             }
04989         }
04990         
04991         /// Enzyme commission numbers specification
04992         if(compound_specification->GetEnzymeCommissionNumbers().size() > 0)
04993         {
04994             vector<string> enzyme_commission_numbers = compound_specification->GetEnzymeCommissionNumbers();
04995             stringstream commission_numbers;
04996             commission_numbers << " EC: ";
04997             for(vector<string>::iterator it1 = enzyme_commission_numbers.begin(); it1 != enzyme_commission_numbers.end(); it1++)
04998             {
04999                 if(it1 < enzyme_commission_numbers.end()-1)
05000                     commission_numbers << (*it1) << ",";
05001                 else
05002                     commission_numbers << (*it1);
05003             }
05004             commission_numbers << ";";
05005             int length = commission_numbers.str().length();
05006             if(length <= MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE)
05007             {
05008                 stringstream ss;
05009                 ss << commission_numbers.str();
05010                 stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
05011                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05012                        << right << setw(3) << counter
05013                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
05014                 counter++;
05015             }
05016             else
05017             {
05018                 int number_of_lines = ceil((double)(length) / MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
05019                 for(int i = 1; i <= number_of_lines; i++)
05020                 {
05021                     if(i != number_of_lines)
05022                     {
05023                         stringstream ss;
05024                         ss << commission_numbers.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
05025                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
05026                                << left << setw(1) << " "
05027                                << right << setw(3) << counter
05028                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
05029                         counter++;
05030                     }
05031                     else
05032                     {
05033                         stringstream ss;
05034                         ss << commission_numbers.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, length - (i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
05035                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
05036                                << left << setw(1) << " "
05037                                << right << setw(3) << counter
05038                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
05039                         counter++;
05040                     }
05041                 }
05042             }
05043         }
05044         
05045         /// Engineered specification
05046         if(compound_specification->GetIsEngineered())
05047         {
05048             stringstream ss;
05049             ss << " ENGINEERED: YES;";
05050             stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
05051                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05052                    << right << setw(3) << counter
05053                    << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
05054             counter++;
05055         }
05056         
05057         /// Mutation specification
05058         if(compound_specification->GetHasMutation())
05059         {
05060             stringstream ss;
05061             ss << " MUTATION: YES;";
05062             stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
05063                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05064                    << right << setw(3) << counter
05065                    << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
05066             counter++;
05067         }
05068         
05069         /// Other comments specification
05070         if(compound_specification->GetComments() != "")
05071         {
05072             stringstream comments;
05073             comments << " OTHER_DETAILS: " << compound_specification->GetComments() << ";";
05074             int length = comments.str().length();
05075             if(length <= MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE)
05076             {
05077                 stringstream ss;
05078                 ss << comments.str();
05079                 stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
05080                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05081                        << right << setw(3) << counter
05082                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
05083                 counter++;
05084             }
05085             else
05086             {
05087                 int number_of_lines = ceil((double)(length) / MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
05088                 for(int i = 1; i <= number_of_lines; i++)
05089                 {
05090                     if(i != number_of_lines)
05091                     {
05092                         stringstream ss;
05093                         ss << comments.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
05094                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
05095                                << left << setw(1) << " "
05096                                << right << setw(3) << counter
05097                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
05098                         counter++;
05099                     }
05100                     else
05101                     {
05102                         stringstream ss;
05103                         ss << comments.str().substr((i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE, length - (i-1)*MAX_LENGTH_OF_COMPOUND_SPEC_IN_LINE);
05104                         stream << left << setw(6) << compound_->GetRecordName()
05105                                << left << setw(1) << " "
05106                                << right << setw(3) << counter
05107                                << left << setw(70) << ss.str() << endl;
05108                         counter++;
05109                     }
05110                 }
05111             }
05112         }
05113         
05114         first = false;
05115         
05116     }
05117     
05118 }

05135 void PdbFile::ResolveNumModelCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05136 {
05137     stream << left << setw(6) << number_of_models_->GetRecordName()
05138            << left << setw(4) << " ";
05139     if(number_of_models_->GetNumberOfModels() != iNotSet)
05140         stream << right << setw(4) << number_of_models_->GetNumberOfModels();
05141     else
05142         stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05143     stream << left << setw(66) << " "
05144            << endl;
05145 }
05146 
05147 void PdbFile::ResolveModelTypeCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05148 {
05149     stream << left << setw(6) << model_type_->GetRecordName()
05150            << left << setw(2) << " ";
05151     stringstream ss;
05152     for(vector<string>::iterator it = model_type_->GetComments().begin(); it != model_type_->GetComments().end(); it++)
05153     {
05154         if(it != model_type_->GetComments().end() - 1)
05155         {
05156             ss << (*it) << "; ";
05157         }
05158         else
05159         {
05160             ss << (*it);
05161         }
05162     }
05163     if(ss.str().length() > 70)
05164     {
05165         stream << right << setw(2) << " "
05166                << left << setw(70) << ss.str().substr(0,70)
05167                << endl;
05168         
05169         int counter = ceil((double)(ss.str().length()) / 70);
05170         for(int i = 2; i <= counter; i++)
05171         {
05172             if(i != counter)
05173             {
05174                 stream << left << setw(6) << model_type_->GetRecordName()
05175                        << left << setw(2) << " "
05176                        << right << setw(2) << i
05177                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str().substr(70*(i-1), 70)
05178                        << endl;
05179             }
05180             else
05181             {
05182                 stream << left << setw(6) << model_type_->GetRecordName()
05183                        << left << setw(2) << " "
05184                        << right << setw(2) << i
05185                        << left << setw(70) << ss.str().substr(70*(i-1), ss.str().length() - (i-1)*70)
05186                        << endl;
05187             }
05188         }
05189     }
05190     else
05191     {
05192         stream << right << setw(2) << " "
05193                << left << setw(70) << ss.str()
05194                << endl;
05195     }
05196 }

05233 void PdbFile::ResolveSequenceResidueCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05234 {
05235     PdbResidueSequenceCard::ResidueSequenceMap residue_sequence_map = residues_sequence_->GetResidueSequenceChain();
05236     for(PdbResidueSequenceCard::ResidueSequenceMap::iterator it = residue_sequence_map.begin(); it != residue_sequence_map.end(); it++)
05237     {
05238         
05239         PdbResidueSequence* residue_sequence = (*it).second;
05240         int serial_number = 1;
05241         const int MAX_RESIDUE_IN_SINGLE_LINE = 13;
05242         vector<string> residue_names = residue_sequence->GetResidueNames();
05243         if(residue_sequence->GetNumberOfResidues() <= MAX_RESIDUE_IN_SINGLE_LINE)
05244         {
05245             stringstream ss;
05246             for(vector<string>::iterator it1 = residue_names.begin(); it1 != residue_names.end(); it1++)
05247             {
05248                 ss << right << setw(1) << " "
05249                    << right << setw(3) << (*it1);
05250             }
05251             for(int i = 0; i < MAX_RESIDUE_IN_SINGLE_LINE - residue_sequence->GetNumberOfResidues(); i++)
05252             {
05253                 ss << right << setw(1) << " "
05254                    << right << setw(3) << " ";
05255             }
05256             stream << left << setw(6) << residues_sequence_->GetRecordName()
05257                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05258                    << right << setw(3) << serial_number
05259                    << right << setw(1) << " "
05260                    << right << setw(1) << residue_sequence->GetChainId()
05261                    << right << setw(1) << " ";
05262             if(residue_sequence->GetNumberOfResidues() != iNotSet)
05263                 stream << right << setw(4) << residue_sequence->GetNumberOfResidues();
05264             else
05265                 stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05266             stream << right << setw(1) << " "
05267                    << right << setw(52) << ss.str()
05268                    << right << setw(10) << " "
05269                    << endl;
05270         }
05271         else
05272         {
05273             int number_of_lines = ceil((double)(residue_sequence->GetNumberOfResidues()) / MAX_RESIDUE_IN_SINGLE_LINE);
05274             for(int i = 0; i < number_of_lines; i++)
05275             {
05276                 stringstream ss;
05277                 if(i != number_of_lines - 1)
05278                 {
05279                     for(vector<string>::iterator it1 = residue_names.begin() + i * MAX_RESIDUE_IN_SINGLE_LINE;
05280                         it1 != residue_names.begin() + (i+1) * MAX_RESIDUE_IN_SINGLE_LINE; it1++)
05281                     {
05282                         ss << right << setw(1) << " "
05283                            << right << setw(3) << (*it1);
05284                     }
05285                 }
05286                 else
05287                 {
05288                     for(vector<string>::iterator it1 = residue_names.begin() + i * MAX_RESIDUE_IN_SINGLE_LINE;
05289                         it1 != residue_names.end(); it1++)
05290                     {
05291                         ss << right << setw(1) << " "
05292                            << right << setw(3) << (*it1);
05293                     }
05294                     for(int i = 0; i < MAX_RESIDUE_IN_SINGLE_LINE - residue_sequence->GetNumberOfResidues() % MAX_RESIDUE_IN_SINGLE_LINE; i++)
05295                     {
05296                         ss << right << setw(1) << " "
05297                            << right << setw(3) << " ";
05298                     }
05299                 }
05300                 stream << left << setw(6) << residues_sequence_->GetRecordName()
05301                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05302                        << right << setw(3) << serial_number
05303                        << right << setw(1) << " "
05304                        << right << setw(1) << residue_sequence->GetChainId()
05305                        << right << setw(1) << " ";
05306                 if(residue_sequence->GetNumberOfResidues() != iNotSet)
05307                     stream << right << setw(4) << residue_sequence->GetNumberOfResidues();
05308                 else
05309                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05310                 stream << right << setw(1) << " "
05311                        << right << setw(52) << ss.str()
05312                        << right << setw(10) << " "
05313                        << endl;
05314                 serial_number++;
05315             }
05316         }
05317         
05318     }
05319 }

05321 void PdbFile::ResolveModificationResidueCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05322 {
05323     PdbResidueModificationCard::ResidueModificationMap residue_modification_map = residue_modification_->GetResidueModifications();
05324     for(PdbResidueModificationCard::ResidueModificationMap::iterator it = residue_modification_map.begin(); it != residue_modification_map.end(); it++)
05325     {
05326         PdbResidueModification* residue_modification = (*it).second;
05327         stream << left << setw(6) << residue_modification_->GetRecordName()
05328                << left << setw(1) << " "
05329                << right << setw(4) << residue_modification->GetIdCode()
05330                << left << setw(1) << " "
05331                << right << setw(3) << residue_modification->GetResidueName()
05332                << left << setw(1) << " "
05333                << right << setw(1) << residue_modification->GetChainId()
05334                << left << setw(1) << " ";
05335         if(residue_modification->GetSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05336             stream << right << setw(4) << residue_modification->GetSequenceNumber();
05337         else
05338             stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05339         stream << right << setw(1) << residue_modification->GetInsertionCode()
05340                << left << setw(1) << " "
05341                << right << setw(3) << residue_modification->GetStandardResidueName()
05342                << left << setw(2) << " "
05343                << left << setw(41) << residue_modification->GetDscr()
05344                << left << setw(10) << " "
05345                << endl;
05346     }
05347 }

05349 void PdbFile::ResolveHeterogenCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05350 {
05351     PdbHeterogenCard::HeterogenMap heterogen_map = heterogens_->GetHeterogens();
05352     for(PdbHeterogenCard::HeterogenMap::iterator it = heterogen_map.begin(); it != heterogen_map.end(); it++)
05353     {
05354         
05355         PdbHeterogen* heterogen = (*it).second;
05356         stream << left << setw(6) << heterogens_->GetRecordName()
05357                << left << setw(1) << " "
05358                << right << setw(3) << heterogen->GetHeterogenId()
05359                << left << setw(2) << " "
05360                << right << setw(1) << heterogen->GetChainId();
05361         if(heterogen->GetSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05362             stream << right << setw(4) << heterogen->GetSequenceNumber();
05363         else
05364             stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05365         stream << right << setw(1) << heterogen->GetInsertionCode()
05366                << left << setw(2) << " ";
05367         if(heterogen->GetNumberOfHeterogenAtoms() != iNotSet)
05368             stream << right << setw(5) << heterogen->GetNumberOfHeterogenAtoms();
05369         else
05370             stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
05371         stream << left << setw(5) << " "
05372                << left << setw(40) << heterogen->GetDscr()
05373                << left << setw(10) << " "
05374                << endl;
05375     }
05376 }

05378 void PdbFile::ResolveHeterogenNameCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05379 {
05380     PdbHeterogenNameCard::HeterogenNameMap heterogen_name_map = heterogens_name_->GetHeterogenNames();
05381     for(PdbHeterogenNameCard::HeterogenNameMap::iterator it = heterogen_name_map.begin(); it != heterogen_name_map.end(); it++)
05382     {
05383         PdbHeterogenName* heterogen_name = (*it).second;
05384         const int MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE = 55;
05385         if((int)heterogen_name->GetHeterogenName().length() > MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05386         {
05387             stream << left << setw(6) << heterogens_name_->GetRecordName()
05388                    << left << setw(2) << " "
05389                    << right << setw(2) << " "
05390                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05391                    << right << setw(3) << heterogen_name->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05392                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05393                    << left << setw(55) << heterogen_name->GetHeterogenName().substr(0,MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05394                    << left << setw(10) << " "
05395                    << endl;
05396             int counter = ceil((double)(heterogen_name->GetHeterogenName().length()) / MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE);
05397             for(int i = 2; i <= counter; i++)
05398             {
05399                 if(i != counter)
05400                 {
05401                     stream << left << setw(6) << heterogens_name_->GetRecordName()
05402                            << left << setw(2) << " "
05403                            << right << setw(2) << i
05404                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05405                            << right << setw(3) << heterogen_name->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05406                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05407                            << left << setw(55) << heterogen_name->GetHeterogenName().substr(MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1),MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05408                            << left << setw(10) << " "
05409                            << endl;
05410                 }
05411                 else
05412                 {
05413                     stream << left << setw(6) << heterogens_name_->GetRecordName()
05414                            << left << setw(2) << " "
05415                            << right << setw(2) << i
05416                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05417                            << right << setw(3) << heterogen_name->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05418                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05419                            << left << setw(55) << heterogen_name->GetHeterogenName().substr(MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1),heterogen_name->GetHeterogenName().length()-MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1))
05420                            << left << setw(10) << " "
05421                            << endl;
05422                 }
05423             }
05424         }
05425         else
05426         {
05427             stream << left << setw(6) << heterogens_name_->GetRecordName()
05428                    << left << setw(2) << " "
05429                    << right << setw(2) << " "
05430                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05431                    << right << setw(3) << heterogen_name->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05432                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05433                    << left << setw(55) << heterogen_name->GetHeterogenName()
05434                    << left << setw(10) << " "
05435                    << endl;
05436         }
05437     }

05440 void PdbFile::ResolveHeterogenSynonymCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05441 {
05442     PdbHeterogenSynonymCard::HeterogenSynonymMap heterogen_synonym_map = heterogen_synonyms_->GetHeterogensSynonyms();
05443     for(PdbHeterogenSynonymCard::HeterogenSynonymMap::iterator it = heterogen_synonym_map.begin(); it != heterogen_synonym_map.end(); it++)
05444     {
05445         PdbHeterogenSynonym* heterogen_synonym = (*it).second;
05446         stringstream ss;
05447         vector<string> synonyms = heterogen_synonym->GetHeterogenSynonyms();
05448         for(vector<string>::iterator it = synonyms.begin(); it != synonyms.end(); it++)
05449         {
05450             if(it != synonyms.end() - 1)
05451             {
05452                 ss << (*it) << "; ";
05453             }
05454             else
05455             {
05456                 ss << (*it) << ";";
05457             }
05458         }
05459         const int MAX_SYNONYM_LENGTH_IN_LINE = 55;
05460         if((int)ss.str().length() > MAX_SYNONYM_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05461         {
05462             stream << left << setw(6) << heterogen_synonyms_->GetRecordName()
05463                    << left << setw(2) << " "
05464                    << right << setw(2) << " "
05465                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05466                    << right << setw(3) << heterogen_synonym->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05467                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05468                    << left << setw(55) << ss.str().substr(0,MAX_SYNONYM_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05469                    << left << setw(10) << " "
05470                    << endl;
05471             int counter = ceil((double)(ss.str().length()) / MAX_SYNONYM_LENGTH_IN_LINE);
05472             for(int i = 2; i <= counter; i++)
05473             {
05474                 if(i != counter)
05475                 {
05476                     stream << left << setw(6) << heterogen_synonyms_->GetRecordName()
05477                            << left << setw(2) << " "
05478                            << right << setw(2) << i
05479                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05480                            << right << setw(3) << heterogen_synonym->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05481                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05482                            << left << setw(55) << ss.str().substr(MAX_SYNONYM_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1),MAX_SYNONYM_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05483                            << left << setw(10) << " "
05484                            << endl;
05485                 }
05486                 else
05487                 {
05488                     stream << left << setw(6) << heterogen_synonyms_->GetRecordName()
05489                            << left << setw(2) << " "
05490                            << right << setw(2) << i
05491                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05492                            << right << setw(3) << heterogen_synonym->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05493                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05494                            << left << setw(55) << ss.str().substr(MAX_SYNONYM_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1),ss.str().length()-MAX_SYNONYM_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1))
05495                            << left << setw(10) << " "
05496                            << endl;
05497                 }
05498             }
05499         }
05500         else
05501         {
05502             stream << left << setw(6) << heterogen_synonyms_->GetRecordName()
05503                    << left << setw(2) << " "
05504                    << right << setw(2) << " "
05505                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05506                    << right << setw(3) << heterogen_synonym->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05507                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05508                    << left << setw(55) << ss.str()
05509                    << left << setw(10) << " "
05510                    << endl;
05511         }
05512     }
05513 }
