05515 void PdbFile::ResolveFormulaCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05516 {
05517     PdbFormulaCard::FormulaMap formula_map = formulas_->GetFormulas();
05518     for(PdbFormulaCard::FormulaMap::iterator it = formula_map.begin(); it != formula_map.end(); it++)
05519     {
05520         PdbFormula* formula = (*it).second;
05521         const int MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE = 51;
05522         if((int)formula->GetChemicalFormula().length() > MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05523         {
05524             stream << left << setw(6) << formulas_->GetRecordName()
05525                    << left << setw(2) << " ";
05526             if(formula->GetComponentNumber() != iNotSet)
05527                 stream << right << setw(2) << formula->GetComponentNumber();
05528             else
05529                 stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05530             stream << left << setw(2) << " "
05531                    << right << setw(3) << formula->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05532                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05533                    << right << setw(2) << " "
05534                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05535                    << left << setw(51) << formula->GetChemicalFormula().substr(0,MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05536                    << left << setw(10) << " "
05537                    << endl;
05538             int counter = ceil((double)(formula->GetChemicalFormula().length()) / MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE);
05539             for(int i = 2; i <= counter; i++)
05540             {
05541                 if(i != counter)
05542                 {
05543                     stream << left << setw(6) << formulas_->GetRecordName()
05544                            << left << setw(2) << " ";
05545                     if(formula->GetComponentNumber() != iNotSet)
05546                         stream << right << setw(2) << formula->GetComponentNumber();
05547                     else
05548                         stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05549                     stream << left << setw(2) << " "
05550                            << right << setw(3) << formula->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05551                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05552                            << right << setw(2) << i
05553                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05554                            << left << setw(51) << formula->GetChemicalFormula().substr(MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1),MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05555                            << left << setw(10) << " "
05556                            << endl;
05557                 }
05558                 else
05559                 {
05560                     stream << left << setw(6) << formulas_->GetRecordName()
05561                            << left << setw(2) << " ";
05562                     if(formula->GetComponentNumber()!= iNotSet)
05563                         stream << right << setw(2) << formula->GetComponentNumber();
05564                     else
05565                         stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05566                     stream << left << setw(2) << " "
05567                            << right << setw(3) << formula->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05568                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05569                            << right << setw(2) << i
05570                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05571                            << left << setw(51) << formula->GetChemicalFormula().substr(MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1),formula->GetChemicalFormula().length()-MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE*(i-1))
05572                            << left << setw(10) << " "
05573                            << endl;
05574                 }
05575             }
05576         }
05577         else
05578         {
05579             stream << left << setw(6) << formulas_->GetRecordName()
05580                    << left << setw(2) << " ";
05581             if(formula->GetComponentNumber() != iNotSet)
05582                 stream << right << setw(2) << formula->GetComponentNumber();
05583             else
05584                 stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05585             stream << left << setw(2) << " "
05586                    << right << setw(3) << formula->GetHeterogenIdentifier()
05587                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05588                    << right << setw(2) << " "
05589                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05590                    << left << setw(51) << formula->GetChemicalFormula().substr(0,MAX_NAME_LENGTH_IN_LINE)
05591                    << left << setw(10) << " "
05592                    << endl;
05593         }
05594     }
05595 }
05596 
05597 void PdbFile::ResolveHelixCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05598 {
05599     PdbHelixCard::HelixMap helix_map = helixes_->GetHelixes();
05600     int counter = helix_map.size();
05601     int serial_number = 1;
05602     while(serial_number <= counter)
05603     {
05604         for(PdbHelixCard::HelixMap::iterator it = helix_map.begin(); it != helix_map.end(); it++)
05605         {
05606             
05607             PdbHelix* helix = (*it).second;
05608             PdbHelix::HelixResidueVector helix_residues = helix->GetHelixResidues();
05609             if(helix->GetHelixSerialNumber() == serial_number)
05610             {
05611                 stream << left << setw(6) << helixes_->GetRecordName()
05612                        << left << setw(1) << " ";
05613                 if(helix->GetHelixSerialNumber() != iNotSet)
05614                     stream << right << setw(3) << helix->GetHelixSerialNumber();
05615                 else
05616                     stream << right << setw(3) << " ";
05617                 stream << left << setw(1) << " "
05618                        << right << setw(3) << helix->GetHelixId()
05619                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05620                        << right << setw(3) << helix_residues.at(0)->GetResidueName()
05621                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05622                        << right << setw(1) << helix_residues.at(0)->GetResidueChainId()
05623                        << left << setw(1) << " ";
05624                 if(helix_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05625                     stream << right << setw(4) << helix_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05626                 else
05627                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05628                 stream << right << setw(1) << helix_residues.at(0)->GetResidueInsertionCode()
05629                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05630                        << right << setw(3) << helix_residues.at(1)->GetResidueName()
05631                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05632                        << right << setw(1) << helix_residues.at(1)->GetResidueChainId()
05633                        << left << setw(1) << " ";
05634                 if(helix_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05635                     stream << right << setw(4) << helix_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05636                 else
05637                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05638                 stream << right << setw(1) << helix_residues.at(1)->GetResidueInsertionCode();
05639                 if(helix->GetHelixClass() != UnknownHelix)
05640                     stream << right << setw(2) << helix->GetHelixClass();
05641                 else
05642                     stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05643                 stream << left << setw(30) << helix->GetComment()
05644                        << left << setw(1) << " ";
05645                 if(helix->GetHelixLength() != dNotSet)
05646                     stream << right << setw(5) << helix->GetHelixLength();
05647                 else
05648                     stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
05649                 stream << left << setw(4) << " "
05650                        << endl;
05651                 break;
05652             }
05653         }
05654         serial_number++;
05655     }
05656 }
05657 
05658 void PdbFile::ResolveSheetCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05659 {
05660     PdbSheetCard::SheetMap sheet_map = sheets_->GetSheets();
05661     for(PdbSheetCard::SheetMap::iterator it = sheet_map.begin(); it != sheet_map.end(); it++)
05662     {
05663         PdbSheet* sheet = (*it).second;
05664         PdbSheet::SheetStrandVector strands = sheet->GetStrands();
05665         int serial_number = 1;
05666         for(PdbSheet::SheetStrandVector::iterator it1 = strands.begin(); it1 != strands.end(); it1++)
05667         {
05668             PdbSheetStrand* strand = (*it1);
05669             PdbSheetStrand::SheetStrandResidueVector strand_residues = strand->GetStrandResidues();
05670             if(strand->GetSense() != 0)
05671             {
05672                 stream << left << setw(6) << sheets_->GetRecordName()
05673                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05674                        << right << setw(3) << serial_number
05675                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05676                        << right << setw(3) << sheet->GetSheetId();
05677                 if(sheet->GetNumberOfStrands() != iNotSet)
05678                     stream << right << setw(2) << sheet->GetNumberOfStrands();
05679                 else
05680                     stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05681                 stream << left << setw(1) << " "
05682                        << right << setw(3) << strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueName()
05683                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05684                        << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueChainId();
05685                 if(strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05686                     stream << right << setw(4) << strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05687                 else
05688                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05689                 stream << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueInsertionCode()
05690                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05691                        << right << setw(3) << strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueName()
05692                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05693                        << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueChainId();
05694                 if(strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05695                     stream << right << setw(4) << strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05696                 else
05697                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05698                 stream << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueInsertionCode();
05699                 if(strand->GetSense() != UnknownStrand)
05700                     stream << right << setw(2) << strand->GetSense();
05701                 else
05702                     stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05703                 stream << left << setw(1) << " "
05704                        << left << setw(4) << strand->GetCurrentAtom()
05705                        << right << setw(3) << strand_residues.at(2)->GetResidueName()
05706                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05707                        << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(2)->GetResidueChainId();
05708                 if(strand_residues.at(2)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05709                     stream << right << setw(4) << strand_residues.at(2)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05710                 else
05711                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05712                 stream << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(2)->GetResidueInsertionCode()
05713                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05714                        << left << setw(4) << strand->GetPreviousAtom()
05715                        << right << setw(3) << strand_residues.at(3)->GetResidueName()
05716                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05717                        << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(3)->GetResidueChainId();
05718                 if(strand_residues.at(3)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05719                     stream << right << setw(4) << strand_residues.at(3)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05720                 else
05721                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05722                 stream << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(3)->GetResidueInsertionCode()
05723                        << left << setw(10) << " "
05724                        << endl;
05725             }
05726             else
05727             {
05728                 stream << left << setw(6) << sheets_->GetRecordName()
05729                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05730                        << right << setw(3) << serial_number
05731                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05732                        << right << setw(3) << sheet->GetSheetId();
05733                 if(sheet->GetNumberOfStrands() != iNotSet)
05734                     stream << right << setw(2) << sheet->GetNumberOfStrands();
05735                 else
05736                     stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05737                 stream << left << setw(1) << " "
05738                        << right << setw(3) << strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueName()
05739                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05740                        << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueChainId();
05741                 if(strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05742                     stream << right << setw(4) << strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05743                 else
05744                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05745                 stream << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(0)->GetResidueInsertionCode()
05746                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05747                        << right << setw(3) << strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueName()
05748                        << left << setw(1) << " "
05749                        << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueChainId();
05750                 if(strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05751                     stream << right << setw(4) << strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05752                 else
05753                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05754                 stream << right << setw(1) << strand_residues.at(1)->GetResidueInsertionCode();
05755                 if(strand->GetSense() != UnknownStrand)
05756                     stream << right << setw(2) << strand->GetSense();
05757                 else
05758                     stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05759                 stream << left << setw(40) << " "
05760                        << endl;
05761             }
05762             serial_number++;
05763         }
05764         
05765     }
05766 }

05768 void PdbFile::ResolveDisulfideBondCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05769 {
05770     PdbDisulfideBondCard::DisulfideResidueBondMap disulfide_bond_map = disulfide_bonds_->GetDisulfideResidueBonds();
05771     for(PdbDisulfideBondCard::DisulfideResidueBondMap::iterator it = disulfide_bond_map.begin(); it != disulfide_bond_map.end(); it++)
05772     {
05773         PdbDisulfideResidueBond* disulfide_bonds = (*it).second;
05774         PdbDisulfideResidueBond::DisulfideResidueVector disulfide_bonds_residues = disulfide_bonds->GetResidues();
05775         stream << left << setw(6) << disulfide_bonds_->GetRecordName()
05776                << left << setw(1) << " ";
05777         if(disulfide_bonds->GetSerialNumber() != iNotSet)
05778             stream << right << setw(3) << disulfide_bonds->GetSerialNumber();
05779         else
05780             stream << right << setw(3) << " ";
05781         stream << left << setw(1) << " "
05782                << right << setw(3) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(0)->GetResidueName()
05783                << left << setw(1) << " "
05784                << right << setw(1) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(0)->GetResidueChainId()
05785                << left << setw(1) << " ";
05786         if(disulfide_bonds_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05787             stream << right << setw(4) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05788         else
05789             stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05790         stream << right << setw(1) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(0)->GetResidueInsertionCode()
05791                << left << setw(3) << " "
05792                << right << setw(3) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(1)->GetResidueName()
05793                << left << setw(1) << " "
05794                << right << setw(1) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(1)->GetResidueChainId()
05795                << left << setw(1) << " ";
05796         if(disulfide_bonds_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05797             stream << right << setw(4) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05798         else
05799             stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05800         stream << right << setw(1) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(1)->GetResidueInsertionCode()
05801                << left << setw(23) << " ";
05802         if(disulfide_bonds_residues.at(0)->GetSymmetryOperator() != iNotSet)
05803             stream << right << setw(6) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(0)->GetSymmetryOperator();
05804         else
05805             stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
05806         stream << left << setw(1) << " ";
05807         if(disulfide_bonds_residues.at(1)->GetSymmetryOperator() != iNotSet)
05808             stream << right << setw(6) << disulfide_bonds_residues.at(1)->GetSymmetryOperator();
05809         else
05810             stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
05811         stream << left << setw(1) << " ";
05812         if(disulfide_bonds->GetBondLength() != dNotSet)
05813             stream << right << setw(5) << fixed << setprecision(2) << disulfide_bonds->GetBondLength();
05814         else
05815             stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
05816         stream << left << setw(2) << " "
05817                << endl;
05818     }
05819 }
05820 
05821 void PdbFile::ResolveLinkCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05822 {
05823     PdbLinkCard::LinkVector links = links_->GetResidueLinks();
05824     for(PdbLinkCard::LinkVector::iterator it = links.begin(); it != links.end(); it++)
05825     {
05826         PdbLink* link = (*it);
05827         PdbLink::LinkResidueVector link_residues = link->GetResidues();
05828         stream << left << setw(6) << links_->GetRecordName()
05829                << left << setw(6) << " "
05830                << left << setw(4) << link_residues.at(0)->GetAtomName()
05831                << right << setw(1) << link_residues.at(0)->GetAlternateLocationIndicator()
05832                << right << setw(3) << link_residues.at(0)->GetResidueName()
05833                << left << setw(1) << " "
05834                << right << setw(1) << link_residues.at(0)->GetResidueChainId();
05835         if(link_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05836             stream << right << setw(4) << link_residues.at(0)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05837         else
05838             stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05839         stream << right << setw(1) << link_residues.at(0)->GetResidueInsertionCode()
05840                << left << setw(15) << " "
05841                << left << setw(4) << link_residues.at(1)->GetAtomName()
05842                << right << setw(1) << link_residues.at(1)->GetAlternateLocationIndicator()
05843                << right << setw(3) << link_residues.at(1)->GetResidueName()
05844                << left << setw(1) << " "
05845                << right << setw(1) << link_residues.at(1)->GetResidueChainId();
05846         if(link_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05847             stream << right << setw(4) << link_residues.at(1)->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05848         else
05849             stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
05850         stream << right << setw(1) << link_residues.at(1)->GetResidueInsertionCode()
05851                << left << setw(2) << " ";
05852         if(link_residues.at(0)->GetSymmetryOperator() != iNotSet)
05853             stream << right << setw(6) << link_residues.at(0)->GetSymmetryOperator();
05854         else
05855             stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
05856         stream << left << setw(1) << " ";
05857         if(link_residues.at(1)->GetSymmetryOperator() != iNotSet)
05858             stream << right << setw(6) << link_residues.at(1)->GetSymmetryOperator();
05859         else
05860             stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
05861         stream << left << setw(1) << " ";
05862         if(link->GetLinkLength() != dNotSet)
05863             stream << right << setw(5) << fixed << setprecision(2) << link->GetLinkLength();
05864         else
05865             stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
05866         stream << left << setw(2) << " "
05867                << endl;
05868     }
05869 }

05873

05875 
05876 void PdbFile::ResolveSiteCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05877 {
05878     PdbSiteCard::PdbSiteMap site_map = sites_->GetResidueSites();
05879     for(PdbSiteCard::PdbSiteMap::iterator it = site_map.begin(); it != site_map.end(); it++)
05880     {
05881         PdbSite* site = (*it).second;
05882         PdbSite::SiteResidueVector site_residues = site->GetResidues();
05883         const int MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE = 4;
05884         const int RESIDUE_LENGHT_IN_LINE = 11;
05885         int number_of_residues = site_residues.size();
05886         
05887         int sequence_number = 1;
05888         if(number_of_residues > MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE)
05889         {
05890             int number_of_lines = ceil((double)(number_of_residues) / MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE);
05891             while(sequence_number <= number_of_lines)
05892             {
05893                 if(sequence_number != number_of_lines)
05894                 {
05895                     stringstream ss;
05896                     for(PdbSite::SiteResidueVector::iterator it1 = site_residues.begin()+(sequence_number - 1)*MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE;
05897                         it1 != site_residues.begin()+(sequence_number)*MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE; it1++)
05898                     {
05899                         PdbSiteResidue* residue = (*it1);
05900                         ss << left << setw(1) << " "
05901                            << right << setw(3) << residue->GetResidueName()
05902                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05903                            << right << setw(1) << residue->GetResidueChainId();
05904                         if(residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05905                             ss << right << setw(4) << residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05906                         else
05907                             ss << right << setw(4) << " ";
05908                         ss << right << setw(1) << residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
05909                     }
05910                     ss << left << setw(19) << " ";
05911                     stream << left << setw(6) << sites_->GetRecordName()
05912                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05913                            << right << setw(3) << sequence_number
05914                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05915                            << right << setw(3) << site->GetSiteId()
05916                            << left << setw(1) << " ";
05917                     if(site->GetNumberOfResidues() != iNotSet)
05918                         stream << right << setw(2) << site->GetNumberOfResidues();
05919                     else
05920                         stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05921                     stream << left << setw(63) << ss.str()
05922                            << endl;
05923                 }
05924                 else
05925                 {
05926                     stringstream ss;
05927                     for(PdbSite::SiteResidueVector::iterator it1 = site_residues.begin()+(sequence_number - 1)*MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE;
05928                         it1 != site_residues.end(); it1++)
05929                     {
05930                         PdbSiteResidue* residue = (*it1);
05931                         ss << left << setw(1) << " "
05932                            << right << setw(3) << residue->GetResidueName()
05933                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05934                            << right << setw(1) << residue->GetResidueChainId();
05935                         if(residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05936                             ss << right << setw(4) << residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05937                         else
05938                             ss << right << setw(4) << " ";
05939                         ss << right << setw(1) << residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
05940                     }
05941                     if((sequence_number*MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE-number_of_residues)*RESIDUE_LENGHT_IN_LINE != 0)
05942                         ss << left << setw((sequence_number*MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE-number_of_residues)*RESIDUE_LENGHT_IN_LINE) << " ";
05943                     ss << left << setw(19) << " ";
05944                     stream << left << setw(6) << sites_->GetRecordName()
05945                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05946                            << right << setw(3) << sequence_number
05947                            << left << setw(1) << " "
05948                            << right << setw(3) << site->GetSiteId()
05949                            << left << setw(1) << " ";
05950                     if(site->GetNumberOfResidues() != iNotSet)
05951                         stream << right << setw(2) << site->GetNumberOfResidues();
05952                     else
05953                         stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05954                     stream << left << setw(63) << ss.str()
05955                            << endl;
05956                 }
05957                 sequence_number++;
05958             }
05959             
05960         }
05961         else
05962         {
05963             stringstream ss;
05964             for(PdbSite::SiteResidueVector::iterator it1 = site_residues.begin(); it1 != site_residues.end(); it1++)
05965             {
05966                 PdbSiteResidue* residue = (*it1);
05967                 ss << left << setw(1) << " "
05968                    << right << setw(3) << residue->GetResidueName()
05969                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05970                    << right << setw(1) << residue->GetResidueChainId();
05971                 if(residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
05972                     ss << right << setw(4) << residue->GetResidueSequenceNumber();
05973                 else
05974                     ss << right << setw(4) << " ";
05975                 ss << right << setw(1) << residue->GetResidueInsertionCode();
05976             }
05977             if((MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE-number_of_residues)*RESIDUE_LENGHT_IN_LINE != 0)
05978                 ss << left << setw((MAX_RESIDUE_IN_LINE-number_of_residues)*RESIDUE_LENGHT_IN_LINE) << " ";
05979             ss << left << setw(19) << " ";
05980             
05981             stream << left << setw(6) << sites_->GetRecordName()
05982                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05983                    << right << setw(3) << sequence_number
05984                    << left << setw(1) << " "
05985                    << right << setw(3) << site->GetSiteId()
05986                    << left << setw(1) << " ";
05987             if(site->GetNumberOfResidues() != iNotSet)
05988                 stream << right << setw(2) << site->GetNumberOfResidues();
05989             else
05990                 stream << right << setw(2) << " ";
05991             stream << left << setw(63) << ss.str()
05992                    << endl;
05993             sequence_number++;
05994         }
05995     }
05996 }
05997 
05998 void PdbFile::ResolveCrystallographyCard(std::ofstream& stream)
05999 {
06000     stream << left << setw(6) << crystallography_->GetRecordName();
06001     if(crystallography_->GetA() != dNotSet)
06002         stream << right << setw(9) << fixed << setprecision(3) << crystallography_->GetA();
06003     else
06004         stream << right << setw(9) << " ";
06005     if(crystallography_->GetB() != dNotSet)
06006         stream << right << setw(9) << fixed << setprecision(3) << crystallography_->GetB();
06007     else
06008         stream << right << setw(9) << " ";
06009     if(crystallography_->GetC() != dNotSet)
06010         stream << right << setw(9) << fixed << setprecision(3) << crystallography_->GetC();
06011     else
06012         stream << right << setw(9) << " ";
06013     if(crystallography_->GetAlpha() != dNotSet)
06014         stream << right << setw(7) << fixed << setprecision(2) << crystallography_->GetAlpha();
06015     else
06016         stream << right << setw(7) << " ";
06017     if(crystallography_->GetBeta() != dNotSet)
06018         stream << right << setw(7) << fixed << setprecision(2) << crystallography_->GetBeta();
06019     else
06020         stream << right << setw(7) << " ";
06021     if(crystallography_->GetGamma() != dNotSet)
06022         stream << right << setw(7) << fixed << setprecision(2) << crystallography_->GetGamma();
06023     else
06024         stream << right << setw(7) << " ";
06025     stream << left << setw(1) << " "
06026            << left << setw(11) << crystallography_->GetSpaceGroup();
06027     if(crystallography_->GetZValue() != iNotSet)
06028         stream << right << setw(4) << crystallography_->GetZValue();
06029     else
06030         stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06031     stream << left << setw(10) << " "
06032            << endl;
06033 }

06035 void PdbFile::ResolveOriginCard(std::ofstream& stream)
06036 {
06037     PdbOriginXnCard::OriginXnVector origins = origins_->GetOriginXN();
06038     for(PdbOriginXnCard::OriginXnVector::iterator it = origins.begin(); it != origins.end(); it++)
06039     {
06040         PdbOriginXn* origin = (*it);
06041         stringstream ss;
06042         ss << origin->GetRecordName() << origin->GetN();
06043         stream << left << setw(6) << ss.str()
06044                << left << setw(4) << " ";
06045         if(origin->GetOrigin().CompareTo(Geometry::Coordinate(dNotSet, dNotSet, dNotSet)) == false)
06046         {
06047             stream << right << setw(10) << fixed << setprecision(6) << origin->GetOrigin().GetX()
06048                    << right << setw(10) << fixed << setprecision(6) << origin->GetOrigin().GetY()
06049                    << right << setw(10) << fixed << setprecision(6) << origin->GetOrigin().GetZ();
06050         }
06051         else
06052         {
06053             stream << right << setw(10) << " "
06054                    << right << setw(10) << " "
06055                    << right << setw(10) << " ";
06056         }
06057         
06058         stream << left << setw(5) << " ";
06059         if(origin->GetT() != dNotSet)
06060             stream << right << setw(10) << fixed << setprecision(5) << origin->GetT();
06061         else
06062             stream << right << setw(10) << " ";
06063         stream << left << setw(25) << " "
06064                << endl;
06065     }
06066 }

06100 void PdbFile::ResolveMatrixCard(std::ofstream& stream)
06101 {
06102     PdbMatrixNCard::MatrixNVectorVector matrices = matrices_->GetMatrixN();
06103     int number_of_matrix_entries = matrices.at(0).size();
06104     for(int i = 0; i < number_of_matrix_entries; i++)
06105     {
06106         for(unsigned int j = 0; j < 3; j++)
06107         {
06108             PdbMatrixNCard::MatrixNVector matrix_vector = matrices.at(j);
06109             PdbMatrixN* matrix = matrix_vector.at(i);
06110             stringstream ss;
06111             ss << matrix->GetRecordName() << matrix->GetN();
06112             stream << left << setw(6) << ss.str()
06113                    << left << setw(1) << " ";
06114             if(matrix->GetSerialNumber() != iNotSet)
06115                 stream << right << setw(3) << matrix->GetSerialNumber();
06116             else
06117                 stream << right << setw(3) << " ";
06118             if(matrix->GetTransformationVector().CompareTo(Geometry::Coordinate(dNotSet, dNotSet, dNotSet)) == false)
06119             {
06120                 stream << right << setw(10) << fixed << setprecision(6) << matrix->GetTransformationVector().GetX()
06121                        << right << setw(10) << fixed << setprecision(6) << matrix->GetTransformationVector().GetY()
06122                        << right << setw(10) << fixed << setprecision(6) << matrix->GetTransformationVector().GetZ();
06123             }
06124             else
06125             {
06126                 stream << right << setw(10) << " "
06127                        << right << setw(10) << " "
06128                        << right << setw(10) << " ";
06129             }
06130             stream << left << setw(5) << " ";
06131             if(matrix->GetV() != dNotSet)
06132                 stream << right << setw(10) << fixed << setprecision(5) << matrix->GetV();
06133             else
06134                 stream << right << setw(10) << " ";
06135             stream << left << setw(4) << " ";
06136             if(matrix->GetIGiven() != iNotSet)
06137                 stream << right << setw(1) << matrix->GetIGiven();
06138             else
06139                 stream << right << setw(1) << " ";
06140             stream << left << setw(20) << " "
06141                    << endl;
06142         }
06143     }
06144     
06145 }
06146 
06147 void PdbFile::ResolveModelCard(std::ofstream& stream)
06148 {
06149     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
06150     int number_of_models = models.size();
06151     if(number_of_models == 1)
06152     {
06153         for(PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap::iterator it = models.begin(); it != models.end(); it++)
06154         {
06155             PdbModel* model = (*it).second;
06156             PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
06157             PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
06158             for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
06159             {
06160                 PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
06161                 int serial_number = 0;
06162                 string residue_name = "";
06163                 char chain_id = ' ';
06164                 int residue_sequence_number = 0;
06165                 char insertion_code = ' ';
06166                 PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
06167                 int atoms_size = atoms.size();
06168                 for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
06169                 {
06170                     PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
06171                     stream << left << setw(6) << atom_card->GetRecordName();
06172                     if(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber() != iNotSet)
06173                         stream << right << setw(5) << atom->GetAtomSerialNumber();
06174                     else
06175                         stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06176                     stream << left << setw(1) << " "
06177                            << left << setw(4) << atom->GetAtomName()
06178                            << left << setw(1) << atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation()
06179                            << right << setw(3) << atom->GetAtomResidueName()
06180                            << left << setw(1) << " "
06181                            << left << setw(1) << atom->GetAtomChainId();
06182                     if(atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
06183                         stream << right << setw(4) << atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
06184                     else
06185                         stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06186                     stream << left << setw(1) << atom->GetAtomInsertionCode()
06187                            << left << setw(3) << " ";
06188                     if(atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().CompareTo(Geometry::Coordinate(dNotSet, dNotSet, dNotSet)) == false)
06189                     {
06190                         stream << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetX()
06191                                << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetY()
06192                                << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetZ();
06193                     }
06194                     else
06195                     {
06196                         stream << right << setw(8) << " "
06197                                << right << setw(8) << " "
06198                                << right << setw(8) << " ";
06199                     }
06200                     if(atom->GetAtomOccupancy() != dNotSet)
06201                         stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << atom->GetAtomOccupancy();
06202                     else
06203                         stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06204                     if(atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor() != dNotSet)
06205                         stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor();
06206                     else
06207                         stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06208                     stream << left << setw(10) << " "
06209                            << right << setw(2) << atom->GetAtomElementSymbol()
06210                            << left << setw(2) << atom->GetAtomCharge()
06211                            << endl;
06212                     serial_number = atom->GetAtomSerialNumber();
06213                     residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
06214                     chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
06215                     residue_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
06216                 }
06217                 if(atoms_size != 0)
06218                 {
06219                     stream << left << setw(6) << "TER";
06220                     if(serial_number != iNotSet)
06221                         stream << right << setw(5) << (serial_number+1);
06222                     else
06223                         stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06224                     stream << left << setw(6) << " "
06225                            << right << setw(3) << residue_name
06226                            << left << setw(1) << " "
06227                            << left << setw(1) << chain_id;
06228                     if(residue_sequence_number != iNotSet)
06229                         stream << right << setw(4) << residue_sequence_number;
06230                     else
06231                         stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06232                     stream << left << setw(1) << insertion_code
06233                            << left << setw(53) << " "
06234                            << endl;
06235                 }
06236             }
06237             PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
06238             for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
06239             {
06240                 PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
06241                 PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
06242                 for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
06243                 {
06244                     PdbAtom* heterogen_atom = (*it2).second;
06245                     stream << left << setw(6) << heterogen_atom_card->GetRecordName();
06246                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomSerialNumber() != iNotSet)
06247                         stream << right << setw(5) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomSerialNumber();
06248                     else
06249                         stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06250                     stream << left << setw(1) << " "
06251                            << left << setw(4) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomName()
06252                            << left << setw(1) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation()
06253                            << right << setw(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueName()
06254                            << left << setw(1) << " "
06255                            << left << setw(1) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomChainId();
06256                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
06257                         stream << right << setw(4) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
06258                     else
06259                         stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06260                     stream << left << setw(1) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomInsertionCode()
06261                            << left << setw(3) << " ";
06262                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().CompareTo(Geometry::Coordinate(dNotSet, dNotSet, dNotSet)) == false)
06263                     {
06264                         stream << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetX()
06265                                << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetY()
06266                                << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetZ();
06267                     }
06268                     else
06269                     {
06270                         stream << right << setw(8) << " "
06271                                << right << setw(8) << " "
06272                                << right << setw(8) << " ";
06273                     }
06274                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomOccupancy() != dNotSet)
06275                         stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOccupancy();
06276                     else
06277                         stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06278                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor() != dNotSet)
06279                         stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor();
06280                     else
06281                         stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06282                     stream << left << setw(10) << " "
06283                            << right << setw(2) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomElementSymbol()
06284                            << left << setw(2) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomCharge()
06285                            << endl;
06286                 }
06287             }
06288         }
06289     }
06290     else
06291     {
06292         for(PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap::iterator it = models.begin(); it != models.end(); it++)
06293         {
06294             PdbModel* model = (*it).second;
06295             stream << left << setw(6) << models_->GetRecordName()
06296                    << left << setw(4) << " ";
06297             if(model->GetModelSerialNumber() != iNotSet)
06298                 stream << right << setw(4) << model->GetModelSerialNumber();
06299             else
06300                 stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06301             stream << left << setw(66) << " "
06302                    << endl;
06303             PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
06304             PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
06305             for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
06306             {
06307                 PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
06308                 int serial_number = 0;
06309                 string residue_name = "";
06310                 char chain_id = ' ';
06311                 int residue_sequence_number = 0;
06312                 char insertion_code = ' ';
06313                 PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
06314                 int atoms_size = atoms.size();
06315                 for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
06316                 {
06317                     PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
06318                     stream << left << setw(6) << atom_card->GetRecordName();
06319                     if(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber() != iNotSet)
06320                         stream << right << setw(5) << atom->GetAtomSerialNumber();
06321                     else
06322                         stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06323                     stream << left << setw(1) << " "
06324                            << left << setw(4) << atom->GetAtomName()
06325                            << left << setw(1) << atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation()
06326                            << right << setw(3) << atom->GetAtomResidueName()
06327                            << left << setw(1) << " "
06328                            << left << setw(1) << atom->GetAtomChainId();
06329                     if(atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
06330                         stream << right << setw(4) << atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
06331                     else
06332                         stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06333                     stream << left << setw(1) << atom->GetAtomInsertionCode()
06334                            << left << setw(3) << " ";
06335                     if(atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().CompareTo(Geometry::Coordinate(dNotSet, dNotSet, dNotSet)) == false)
06336                         stream << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetX()
06337                                << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetY()
06338                                << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetZ();
06339                     else
06340                         stream << right << setw(8) << " "
06341                                << right << setw(8) << " "
06342                                << right << setw(8) << " ";
06343                     if(atom->GetAtomOccupancy() != dNotSet)
06344                         stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << atom->GetAtomOccupancy();
06345                     else
06346                         stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06347                     if(atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor() != dNotSet)
06348                         stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor();
06349                     else
06350                         stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06351                     stream << left << setw(10) << " "
06352                            << right << setw(2) << atom->GetAtomElementSymbol()
06353                            << left << setw(2) << atom->GetAtomCharge()
06354                            << endl;
06355                     serial_number = atom->GetAtomSerialNumber();
06356                     residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
06357                     chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
06358                     residue_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
06359                 }
06360                 if(atoms_size != 0)
06361                 {
06362                     stream << left << setw(6) << "TER";
06363                     if(serial_number != iNotSet)
06364                         stream << right << setw(5) << (serial_number+1);
06365                     else
06366                         stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06367                     stream << left << setw(6) << " "
06368                            << right << setw(3) << residue_name
06369                            << left << setw(1) << " "
06370                            << left << setw(1) << chain_id;
06371                     if(residue_sequence_number != iNotSet)
06372                         stream << right << setw(4) << residue_sequence_number;
06373                     else
06374                         stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06375                     stream << left << setw(1) << insertion_code
06376                            << left << setw(53) << " "
06377                            << endl;
06378                 }
06379             }
06380             PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
06381             for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
06382             {
06383                 PdbHeterogenAtomCard* heterogen_atom_card = (*it1);
06384                 PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap heterogen_atoms = heterogen_atom_card->GetHeterogenAtoms();
06385                 for(PdbHeterogenAtomCard::PdbHeterogenAtomMap::iterator it2 = heterogen_atoms.begin(); it2 != heterogen_atoms.end(); it2++)
06386                 {
06387                     PdbAtom* heterogen_atom = (*it2).second;
06388                     stream << left << setw(6) << heterogen_atom_card->GetRecordName();
06389                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomSerialNumber() != iNotSet)
06390                         stream << right << setw(5) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomSerialNumber();
06391                     else
06392                         stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06393                     stream << left << setw(1) << " "
06394                            << left << setw(4) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomName()
06395                            << left << setw(1) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation()
06396                            << right << setw(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueName()
06397                            << left << setw(1) << " "
06398                            << left << setw(1) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomChainId();
06399                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
06400                         stream << right << setw(4) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
06401                     else
06402                         stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06403                     stream << left << setw(1) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomInsertionCode()
06404                            << left << setw(3) << " ";
06405                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().CompareTo(Geometry::Coordinate(dNotSet, dNotSet, dNotSet)) == false)
06406                         stream << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetX()
06407                                << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetY()
06408                                << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetZ();
06409                     else
06410                         stream << right << setw(8) << " "
06411                                << right << setw(8) << " "
06412                                << right << setw(8) << " ";
06413                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomOccupancy() != dNotSet)
06414                         stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOccupancy();
06415                     else
06416                         stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06417                     if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor() != dNotSet)
06418                         stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor();
06419                     else
06420                         stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06421                     stream << left << setw(10) << " "
06422                            << right << setw(2) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomElementSymbol()
06423                            << left << setw(2) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomCharge()
06424                            << endl;
06425                 }
06426             }
06427             stream << left << setw(6) << "ENDMDL"
06428                    << left << setw(74) << " "
06429                    << endl;
06430         }
06431     }
06432 }

06434 void PdbFile::ResolveModelCardWithTheGivenModelNumber(std::ofstream& stream, int model_number)
06435 {
06436     PdbModelCard::PdbModelMap models = models_->GetModels();
06437     if(models.size() != 0)
06438     {
06439         PdbModel* model = models[model_number];
06440         PdbModelResidueSet* residue_set = model->GetModelResidueSet();
06441         PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector atom_cards = residue_set->GetAtoms();
06442         for(PdbModelResidueSet::AtomCardVector::iterator it1 = atom_cards.begin(); it1 != atom_cards.end(); it1++)
06443         {
06444             PdbAtomCard* atom_card = (*it1);
06445             int serial_number = 0;
06446             string residue_name = "";
06447             char chain_id = ' ';
06448             int residue_sequence_number = 0;
06449             char insertion_code = ' ';
06450             PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap atoms = atom_card->GetAtoms();
06451             int atoms_size = atoms.size();
06452             for(PdbAtomCard::PdbAtomMap::iterator it2 = atoms.begin(); it2 != atoms.end(); it2++)
06453             {
06454                 PdbAtom* atom = (*it2).second;
06455                 stream << left << setw(6) << atom_card->GetRecordName();
06456                 if(atom->GetAtomSerialNumber() != iNotSet)
06457                     stream << right << setw(5) << atom->GetAtomSerialNumber();
06458                 else
06459                     stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06460                 stream << left << setw(1) << " "
06461                        << left << setw(4) << atom->GetAtomName()
06462                        << left << setw(1) << atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation()
06463                        << right << setw(3) << atom->GetAtomResidueName()
06464                        << left << setw(1) << " "
06465                        << left << setw(1) << atom->GetAtomChainId();
06466                 if(atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)
06467                     stream << right << setw(4) << atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
06468                 else
06469                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06470                 stream << left << setw(1) << atom->GetAtomInsertionCode()
06471                        << left << setw(3) << " ";
06472                 if(atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().CompareTo(Geometry::Coordinate(dNotSet, dNotSet, dNotSet)) == false)
06473                 {
06474                     stream << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetX()
06475                            << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetY()
06476                            << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetZ();
06477                 }
06478                 else
06479                 {
06480                     stream << right << setw(8) << " "
06481                            << right << setw(8) << " "
06482                            << right << setw(8) << " ";
06483                 }
06484                 if(atom->GetAtomOccupancy() != dNotSet)
06485                     stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << atom->GetAtomOccupancy();
06486                 else
06487                     stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06488                 if(atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor() != dNotSet)
06489                     stream << right << setw(6) << fixed << setprecision(2) << atom->GetAtomTempretureFactor();
06490                 else
06491                     stream << right << setw(6) << " ";
06492                 stream << left << setw(10) << " "
06493                        << right << setw(2) << atom->GetAtomElementSymbol()
06494                        << left << setw(2) << atom->GetAtomCharge()
06495                        << endl;
06496                 serial_number = atom->GetAtomSerialNumber();
06497                 residue_name = atom->GetAtomResidueName();
06498                 chain_id = atom->GetAtomChainId();
06499                 residue_sequence_number = atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber();
06500             }
06501             if(atoms_size != 0)
06502             {
06503                 stream << left << setw(6) << "TER";
06504                 if(serial_number != iNotSet)
06505                     stream << right << setw(5) << (serial_number+1);
06506                 else
06507                     stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06508                 stream << left << setw(6) << " "
06509                        << right << setw(3) << residue_name
06510                        << left << setw(1) << " "
06511                        << left << setw(1) << chain_id;
06512                 if(residue_sequence_number != iNotSet)
06513                     stream << right << setw(4) << residue_sequence_number;
06514                 else
06515                     stream << right << setw(4) << " ";
06516                 stream << left << setw(1) << insertion_code
06517                        << left << setw(53) << " "
06518                        << endl;
06519             }
06520         }
06521         PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector heterogen_atom_cards = residue_set->GetHeterogenAtoms();
06522         for(PdbModelResidueSet::HeterogenAtomCardVector::iterator it1 = heterogen_atom_cards.begin(); it1 != heterogen_atom_cards.end(); it1++)
06523         {

06527             {

06531                     stream << right << setw(5) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomSerialNumber();
06532                 else

06535                        << left << setw(4) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomName()
06536                        << left << setw(1) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomAlternateLocation()
06537                        << right << setw(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueName()

06540                 if(heterogen_atom->GetAtomResidueSequenceNumber() != iNotSet)

06547                 {
06548                     stream << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetX()
06549                            << right << setw(8) << fixed << setprecision(3) << heterogen_atom->GetAtomOrthogonalCoordinate().GetY()

06552                 else

06574 
06575 void PdbFile::ResolveConnectivityCard(std::ofstream& stream)
06576 {
06577     PdbConnectCard::BondedAtomsSerialNumbersMap bonded_atoms = connectivities_->GetBondedAtomsSerialNumbers();
06578     for(PdbConnectCard::BondedAtomsSerialNumbersMap::iterator it = bonded_atoms.begin(); it != bonded_atoms.end(); it++)
06579     {
06580         vector<int> bonded_atoms_serial_number = (*it).second;
06581         int source_atom_serial_number = (*it).first;
06582         int number_of_bonded_atoms = bonded_atoms_serial_number.size();
06583         const int MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE = 4;
06584         const int SERIAL_NUMBER_LENGTH = 5;
06585         if(number_of_bonded_atoms <= MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE)
06586         {
06587             stream << left << setw(6) << connectivities_->GetRecordName();
06588             if(source_atom_serial_number != iNotSet)
06589                 stream << right << setw(5) << source_atom_serial_number;
06590             else
06591                 stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06592             for(vector<int>::iterator it1 = bonded_atoms_serial_number.begin(); it1 != bonded_atoms_serial_number.end(); it1++)
06593             {
06594                 int serial_number = (*it1);
06595                 if(serial_number != iNotSet)
06596                     stream << right << setw(5) << serial_number;
06597                 else
06598                     stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06599             }
06600             if((MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE-number_of_bonded_atoms)*SERIAL_NUMBER_LENGTH != 0)
06601                 stream << left << setw((MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE-number_of_bonded_atoms)*SERIAL_NUMBER_LENGTH) << " "
06602                        << left << setw(49) << " "
06603                        << endl;
06604             else
06605                 stream << left << setw(49) << " "
06606                        << endl;
06607         }
06608         else
06609         {
06610             int number_of_lines = ceil((double)(number_of_bonded_atoms) / MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE);
06611             for(int i = 1; i <= number_of_lines; i++)
06612             {
06613                 stream << left << setw(6) << connectivities_->GetRecordName();
06614                 if(source_atom_serial_number != iNotSet)
06615                     stream << right << setw(5) << source_atom_serial_number;
06616                 else
06617                     stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06618                 if(i != number_of_lines)
06619                 {
06620                     for(vector<int>::iterator it1 = bonded_atoms_serial_number.begin() + (i-1) * MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE;
06621                         it1 != bonded_atoms_serial_number.begin() + i * MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE; it1++)
06622                     {
06623                         int serial_number = (*it1);
06624                         if(serial_number != iNotSet)
06625                             stream << right << setw(5) << serial_number;
06626                         else
06627                             stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06628                     }
06629                     stream << left << setw(49) << " "
06630                            << endl;
06631                 }
06632                 else
06633                 {
06634                     for(vector<int>::iterator it1 = bonded_atoms_serial_number.begin() + (i-1) * MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE;
06635                         it1 != bonded_atoms_serial_number.end(); it1++)
06636                     {
06637                         int serial_number = (*it1);
06638                         if(serial_number != iNotSet)
06639                             stream << right << setw(5) << serial_number;
06640                         else
06641                             stream << right << setw(5) << " ";
06642                     }
06643                     if((MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE-(number_of_bonded_atoms-(i-1)*MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE))*SERIAL_NUMBER_LENGTH != 0)
06644                         stream << left << setw((MAX_SERIAL_NUMBER_IN_LINE-number_of_bonded_atoms)*SERIAL_NUMBER_LENGTH) << " "
06645                                << left << setw(49) << " "
06646                                << endl;
06647                     else
06648                         stream << left << setw(49) << " "
06649                                << endl;
06650                 }
06651             }
06652         }
06653     }
06654 }

06661 void PdbFile::ResolveEndCard(std::ofstream& stream)

06663     stream << left << setw(6) << "END" << left << setw(74) << " " << endl;

06670 void PdbFile::Print(ostream &out)
06671 {
06672     if(header_ != NULL)
06673     {
06674         out << "******************************* HEADER *******************************" << endl;
06675         header_->Print(out);
06676     }
06677     if(title_ != NULL)
06678     {
06679         out << "******************************** TITLE *******************************" << endl;
06680         title_->Print(out);
06681     }
06682     if(compound_ != NULL)
06683     {
06684         out << "****************************** COMPOUND ******************************" << endl;
06685         compound_->Print(out);
06686     }
06687     if(number_of_models_ != NULL)
06688     {
06689         out << "************************** NUMBER OF MODELS **************************" << endl;
06690         number_of_models_->Print(out);
06691     }
06692     if(model_type_ != NULL)
06693     {
06694         out << "***************************** MODEL TYPE *****************************" << endl;
06695         model_type_->Print(out);
06696     }
06697     if(residues_sequence_ != NULL)
06698     {
06699         out << "************************** RESIDUE SEQUENCE **************************" << endl;
06700         residues_sequence_->Print(out);
06701     }
06702     if(residue_modification_ != NULL)
06703     {
06704         out << "************************ RESIDUE MODIFICATION ************************" << endl;
06705         residue_modification_->Print(out);
06706     }
06707     if(heterogens_ != NULL)
06708     {
06709         out << "***************************** HETEROGEN ******************************" << endl;
06710         heterogens_->Print(out);
06711     }
06712     if(heterogens_name_ != NULL)
06713     {
06714         out << "*************************** HETEROGEN NAME ***************************" << endl;
06715         heterogens_name_->Print(out);
06716     }
06717     if(heterogen_synonyms_ != NULL)
06718     {
06719         out << "************************** HETEROGEN SYNONYM *************************" << endl;
06720         heterogen_synonyms_->Print(out);
06721     }
06722     if(formulas_ != NULL)
06723     {
06724         out << "******************************* FORMULA ******************************" << endl;
06725         formulas_->Print(out);
06726     }
06727     if(helixes_ != NULL)
06728     {
06729         out << "******************************** HELIX *******************************" << endl;
06730         helixes_->Print(out);
06731     }
06732     if(sheets_ != NULL)
06733     {
06734         out << "******************************** SHEET *******************************" << endl;
06735         sheets_->Print(out);
06736     }
06737     if(disulfide_bonds_ != NULL)
06738     {
06739         out << "*************************** DISULFIDE BOND ***************************" << endl;
06740         disulfide_bonds_->Print(out);
06741     }
06742     if(links_ != NULL)
06743     {
06744         out << "******************************** LINK ********************************" << endl;
06745         links_->Print(out);
06746     }
06747     if(sites_ != NULL)
06748     {
06749         out << "******************************** SITE ********************************" << endl;
06750         sites_->Print(out);
06751     }
06752     if(crystallography_ != NULL)
06753     {
06754         out << "************************** CRYSTALLOGRAPHIC **************************" << endl;
06755         crystallography_->Print(out);
06756     }
06757     if(origins_ != NULL)
06758     {
06759         out << "******************************* ORIGIN *******************************" << endl;
06760         origins_->Print(out);
06761     }
06762     if(scales_ != NULL)
06763     {
06764         out << "******************************** SCALE *******************************" << endl;
06765         scales_->Print(out);
06766     }
06767     if(matrices_ != NULL)
06768     {
06769         out << "******************************* MATRIX *******************************" << endl;
06770         matrices_->Print(out);
06771     }
06772     if(models_ != NULL)
06773     {
06774         out << "******************************* MODEL ********************************" << endl;
06775         models_->Print(out);
06776     }
06777     if(connectivities_ != NULL)
06778     {
06779         out << "******************************* CONNECT ******************************" << endl;
06780         connectivities_->Print(out);
06781     }
06782 }
